# 🗄️ DATABASE MIGRATIONS (database/migrations/)

## `001_create_core_tables.sql` (UP)
```sql
-- Enable required extensions
CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS "uuid-ossp";
CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS "pgcrypto";

-- Core multi-tenant
CREATE TABLE agencies (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  name TEXT NOT NULL,
  branding JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE TABLE users (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  agency_id UUID REFERENCES agencies(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  role TEXT CHECK (role IN ('super_admin','ops','support','guide','pilgrim','family')),
  email TEXT NOT NULL,
  phone TEXT,
  metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  UNIQUE(agency_id, email)
);

CREATE TABLE pilgrims (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  agency_id UUID NOT NULL,
  group_id UUID,
  first_name TEXT NOT NULL,
  last_name TEXT NOT NULL,
  birth_date DATE,
  passport_number TEXT,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE TABLE groups (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  agency_id UUID NOT NULL,
  name TEXT NOT NULL,
  departure_date DATE NOT NULL,
  guide_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Indexes for RLS performance
CREATE INDEX idx_pilgrims_agency_created ON pilgrims(agency_id, created_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_users_agency_role ON users(agency_id, role);
CREATE INDEX idx_groups_agency_departure ON groups(agency_id, departure_date);
```

## `001_create_core_tables.sql` (DOWN)
```sql
DROP INDEX IF EXISTS idx_groups_agency_departure;
DROP INDEX IF EXISTS idx_users_agency_role;
DROP INDEX IF EXISTS idx_pilgrims_agency_created;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS groups;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS pilgrims;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS users;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS agencies;
```

## `002_create_rls_policies.sql` (UP)
```sql
-- Helper function for agency context
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION app.current_agency_id()
RETURNS UUID AS $$
BEGIN
  RETURN NULLIF(current_setting('app.current_agency_id', true), '')::UUID;
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql SECURITY DEFINER;

-- Enable RLS on all tables
ALTER TABLE agencies ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE users ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE pilgrims ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE groups ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

-- Agency isolation policy (apply to all business tables)
CREATE POLICY agency_isolation_policy ON pilgrims
  FOR ALL USING (agency_id = app.current_agency_id())
  WITH CHECK (agency_id = app.current_agency_id());

CREATE POLICY agency_isolation_policy ON groups
  FOR ALL USING (agency_id = app.current_agency_id())
  WITH CHECK (agency_id = app.current_agency_id());

-- Pilgrim self-view exception
CREATE POLICY pilgrim_self_view ON pilgrims
  FOR SELECT USING (
    app.current_agency_id() = agency_id 
    AND id = NULLIF(current_setting('app.current_pilgrim_id', true), '')::UUID
  );
```

## `002_create_rls_policies.sql` (DOWN)
```sql
DROP POLICY IF EXISTS pilgrim_self_view ON pilgrims;
DROP POLICY IF EXISTS agency_isolation_policy ON groups;
DROP POLICY IF EXISTS agency_isolation_policy ON pilgrims;

ALTER TABLE groups DISABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE pilgrims DISABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE users DISABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE agencies DISABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

DROP FUNCTION IF EXISTS app.current_agency_id();
```

## `003_create_audit_tables.sql` (UP)
```sql
-- Document access audit (RGPD traceability)
CREATE TABLE document_access_logs (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  document_id UUID,
  accessed_by_user_id UUID,
  accessed_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  ip_address INET,
  user_agent TEXT
);

-- Analytics events (anonymized)
CREATE TABLE analytics_events (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  agency_id UUID NOT NULL,
  event_name TEXT NOT NULL,
  anonymized_user_hash TEXT,
  properties JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE INDEX idx_analytics_agency_event ON analytics_events(agency_id, event_name, created_at);
```

# Mon Omra — SaaS B2B2C pour Agences Omra/Hajj

## ⚠️ Avant de Commencer

# 1. Cloner et installer
git clone https://github.com/your-org/mon-omra.git
cd mon-omra
npm install

# 2. Configurer variables d'environnement
cp .env.example .env
# Éditer .env avec vos credentials (Supabase, S3, Resend)

npm run db:migrate:up
npm run db:seed

# 4. Lancer développement
npm run dev

npm run test

# E2E (requires staging env)
npm run test:e2e

# Coverage report
npm run test:coverage
```

- Pre-commit hook vérifie secrets accidentels
- CI bloque merge sans tests passing
- DPIA validation label requis pour merge `main`

## RGPD

- DSAR endpoint : `/api/v1/dsar/export` et `/api/v1/dsar/delete`
- Rétention auto : job quotidien supprime documents expirés
- Audit logs : table `document_access_logs` pour traçabilité

### USER
DPIA ca veut dire quoi

### ASSISTANT
**DPIA** = **Data Protection Impact Assessment**  
*(en français : **AIPD** — Analyse d'Impact relative à la Protection des Données)*

---

### 📋 Définition simple

Une **DPIA** est un document obligatoire (RGPD Art. 35) qui permet d'**identifier, évaluer et réduire les risques** liés au traitement de données personnelles, *avant* de lancer un projet.

> C'est l'équivalent d'une "étude d'impact environnemental", mais pour la vie privée des utilisateurs.

---

### 🔍 Pourquoi une DPIA est requise pour **Mon Omra** ?

| Critère RGPD | Application Mon Omra |
|--------------|---------------------|
| **Données sensibles** | Passeport, visa → peuvent révéler origine, religion, statut migratoire |
| **Cible vulnérable** | Pèlerins en situation spirituelle, parfois peu digitaux, dépendants de l'agence |
| **Surveillance / traçabilité** | Logs d'accès documents, géolocalisation potentielle, historique consultations |
| **Nouvelle technologie** | FAQ IA (P1) → risque d'hallucination sur sujets religieux/légaux |

→ **Combinaison = risque élevé** → DPIA **obligatoire** avant traitement.

---

### 📄 Ce que contient une DPIA (simplifié)

```markdown
1. Description du traitement
   • Quelles données ? Pourquoi ? Qui y accède ?

2. Nécessité & proportionnalité
   • Pourquoi ces données sont-elles indispensables ?

3. Évaluation des risques
   • Risque 1 : Fuite de passeports → Impact : usurpation identité
   • Risque 2 : Accès croisé agences → Impact : violation confidentialité
   • etc.

4. Mesures de protection prévues
   • Chiffrement AES-256, RLS PostgreSQL, URLs 15min, audit logs...

5. Consultation parties prenantes
   • DPO, équipe technique, représentants utilisateurs si besoin

6. Validation finale
   • Signature DPO + date + revue annuelle obligatoire
```

---

### 🚦 Pourquoi on bloque le build métier sur la DPIA ?

```
⚠️ Sans DPIA validée :
• Non-conformité RGPD → sanctions CNIL (jusqu'à 4% du CA mondial)
• Risque légal en cas de fuite de documents sensibles
• Perte de confiance des agences et pèlerins

✅ Avec DPIA validée :
• Preuve de diligence raisonnable
• Mesures de sécurité documentées et traçables
• Base pour audits futurs + assurances
```

---

### 🛠️ Chez NOVA SQUAD

- ✅ **Template DPIA fourni** dans `docs/rgpd/dpia-template.md`
- ✅ **Décision prise** : DPIA requise pour Lot 1 (documents sensibles)
- ⏳ **Action requise** : Remplir le template + validation DPO avant premier commit métier

> 📌 **Rappel** : Le scaffolding (structure, types, migrations) est autorisé sans DPIA signée.  
> 🚫 **Seule la logique métier exécutable** (auth réelle, upload documents, RLS appliqué) est bloquée jusqu'à validation.

3. Passe à autre chose et continue le build scaffolding ?

## 3) Code Livrable — Auth + RLS + Middleware

---

### 📁 `packages/api/src/middleware/auth.ts`

```typescript
import { Request, Response, NextFunction } from 'express';
import { createClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js';
import pino from 'pino';
import crypto from 'crypto';

const logger = pino({
  level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
  redact: ['email', 'phone', 'passport_number', 'token', 'authorization'],
});

const supabase = createClient(
  process.env.SUPABASE_URL!,
  process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!
);

export interface AuthUser {
  id: string;
  agency_id: string;
  role: 'super_admin' | 'ops' | 'support' | 'guide' | 'pilgrim' | 'family';
  email: string;
  phone?: string;
  meta Record<string, unknown>;
}

export interface AuthRequest extends Request {
  user?: AuthUser;
  agency_id?: string;
}

/**
 * Hash email for anonymized logging (RGPD compliant)
 */
function hashEmail(email: string): string {
  const salt = process.env.APP_JWT_SALT || 'default-salt-change-me';
  return crypto.createHash('sha256').update(email + salt).digest('hex').slice(0, 16);
}

/**
 * Auth Middleware - Validates JWT and sets user context
 */
export async function authMiddleware(
  req: AuthRequest,
  res: Response,
  next: NextFunction
): Promise<void> {
  const authHeader = req.headers.authorization;

  if (!authHeader || !authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ')) {
    logger.warn({ route: req.path }, 'Missing or invalid authorization header');
    res.status(401).json({
      error: {
        code: 'UNAUTHORIZED',
        message: 'Invalid or missing authorization token',
      },
    });
    return;
  }

  const token = authHeader.substring(7);

  try {
    // Verify token with Supabase
    const { data: { user }, error } = await supabase.auth.getUser(token);

    if (error || !user) {
      logger.warn({ route: req.path, error: error?.message }, 'Invalid token');
      res.status(401).json({
        error: {
          code: 'UNAUTHORIZED',
          message: 'Invalid or expired token',
        },
      });
      return;
    }

    // Fetch user metadata from our database
    const {  userData, error: dbError } = await supabase
      .from('users')
      .select('id, agency_id, role, email, phone, metadata')
      .eq('id', user.id)
      .single();

    if (dbError || !userData) {
      logger.error({ userId: user.id, error: dbError }, 'User not found in database');
      res.status(401).json({
        error: {
          code: 'UNAUTHORIZED',
          message: 'User not found',
        },
      });
      return;
    }

    // Set user context on request
    req.user = userData as AuthUser;
    req.agency_id = userData.agency_id;

    // Log auth success (without PII)
    logger.info({
      userIdHash: hashEmail(userData.email),
      role: userData.role,
      agencyId: userData.agency_id,
      route: req.path,
      method: req.method,
    }, 'User authenticated');

    next();
  } catch (err) {
    logger.error({ error: err }, 'Auth middleware error');
    res.status(500).json({
      error: {
        code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
        message: 'Authentication service unavailable',
      },
    });
  }
}

/**
 * Role-based access control middleware
 */
export function requireRoles(...allowedRoles: AuthUser['role'][]) {
  return (req: AuthRequest, res: Response, next: NextFunction): void => {
    if (!req.user) {
      res.status(401).json({
        error: { code: 'UNAUTHORIZED', message: 'Authentication required' },
      });
      return;
    }

    if (!allowedRoles.includes(req.user.role)) {
      logger.warn({
        userIdHash: hashEmail(req.user.email),
        role: req.user.role,
        requiredRoles: allowedRoles,
        route: req.path,
      }, 'Role access denied');

      res.status(403).json({
        error: {
          code: 'FORBIDDEN',
          message: 'Insufficient permissions',
        },
      });
      return;
    }

    next();
  };
}

/**
 * Resource ownership check (anti-IDOR)
 */
export async function checkResourceOwnership(
  req: AuthRequest,
  res: Response,
  next: NextFunction,
  resourceTable: string,
  resourceId: string
): Promise<void> {
  if (!req.user || !req.agency_id) {
    res.status(401).json({ error: { code: 'UNAUTHORIZED', message: 'Auth required' } });
    return;
  }

  try {
    // Verify resource belongs to user's agency
    const {  resource, error } = await supabase
      .from(resourceTable)
      .select('agency_id')
      .eq('id', resourceId)
      .single();

    if (error || !resource) {
      logger.warn({ resourceId, table: resourceTable }, 'Resource not found');
      res.status(404).json({
        error: { code: 'NOT_FOUND', message: 'Resource not found' },
      });
      return;
    }

    // Check agency isolation
    if (resource.agency_id !== req.agency_id) {
      logger.warn({
        userIdHash: hashEmail(req.user.email),
        userAgencyId: req.agency_id,
        resourceAgencyId: resource.agency_id,
        resourceId,
      }, 'Cross-agency access attempt');

      res.status(403).json({
        error: { code: 'FORBIDDEN', message: 'Access denied to this resource' },
      });
      return;
    }

    // Pilgrim self-view exception
    if (req.user.role === 'pilgrim' && resourceTable === 'pilgrims') {
      const { data: pilgrimData } = await supabase
        .from('pilgrims')
        .select('id')
        .eq('id', resourceId)
        .eq('id', req.user.id) // Pilgrim can only view themselves
        .single();

      if (!pilgrimData) {
        res.status(403).json({
          error: { code: 'FORBIDDEN', message: 'Can only access own profile' },
        });
        return;
      }
    }

    next();
  } catch (err) {
    logger.error({ error: err }, 'Resource ownership check error');
    res.status(500).json({
      error: { code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR', message: 'Authorization check failed' },
    });
  }
}
```

---

### 📁 `packages/api/src/middleware/rate-limit.ts`

```typescript
import { Request, Response, NextFunction } from 'express';
import { createClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js';
import pino from 'pino';

const logger = pino({ level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info' });

const supabase = createClient(
  process.env.SUPABASE_URL!,
  process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!
);

interface RateLimitConfig {
  windowMs: number;
  maxRequests: number;
  keyPrefix: string;
}

const defaultConfig: RateLimitConfig = {
  windowMs: 60000, // 1 minute
  maxRequests: 100,
  keyPrefix: 'api',
};

const magicLinkConfig: RateLimitConfig = {
  windowMs: 60000, // 1 minute
  maxRequests: 5,
  keyPrefix: 'magic_link',
};

/**
 * Get client identifier (IP + user agent hash)
 */
function getClientId(req: Request): string {
  const ip = req.ip || req.socket.remoteAddress || 'unknown';
  const ua = req.headers['user-agent'] || 'unknown';
  return `${ip}-${ua}`;
}

/**
 * Rate limiting middleware with Supabase storage
 */
export function rateLimit(config: RateLimitConfig = defaultConfig) {
  return async (req: Request, res: Response, next: NextFunction): Promise<void> => {
    const clientId = getClientId(req);
    const key = `${config.keyPrefix}:${clientId}`;
    const now = new Date();

    try {
      // Get or create rate limit record
      const {  existing } = await supabase
        .from('rate_limit_state')
        .select('count, window_start')
        .eq('key', key)
        .single();

      if (existing) {
        const windowStart = new Date(existing.window_start);
        const windowEnd = new Date(windowStart.getTime() + config.windowMs);

        if (now > windowEnd) {
          // Window expired, reset
          await supabase
            .from('rate_limit_state')
            .update({ count: 1, window_start: now.toISOString() })
            .eq('key', key);
          next();
        } else if (existing.count >= config.maxRequests) {
          // Rate limit exceeded
          const retryAfter = Math.ceil((windowEnd.getTime() - now.getTime()) / 1000);
          
          logger.warn({
            clientId,
            key,
            count: existing.count,
            max: config.maxRequests,
            route: req.path,
          }, 'Rate limit exceeded');

          res.set('X-RateLimit-Limit', config.maxRequests.toString());
          res.set('X-RateLimit-Remaining', '0');
          res.set('X-RateLimit-Reset', windowEnd.toISOString());
          res.set('Retry-After', retryAfter.toString());

          res.status(429).json({
            error: {
              code: 'RATE_LIMITED',
              message: 'Too many requests',
              details: { retry_after_sec: retryAfter },
            },
          });
        } else {
          // Increment counter
          await supabase
            .from('rate_limit_state')
            .update({ count: existing.count + 1 })
            .eq('key', key);

          res.set('X-RateLimit-Limit', config.maxRequests.toString());
          res.set('X-RateLimit-Remaining', (config.maxRequests - existing.count - 1).toString());
          next();
        }
      } else {
        // Create new record
        await supabase
          .from('rate_limit_state')
          .insert({
            key,
            count: 1,
            window_start: now.toISOString(),
            expires_at: new Date(now.getTime() + 3600000).toISOString(), // 1 hour
          });

        res.set('X-RateLimit-Limit', config.maxRequests.toString());
        res.set('X-RateLimit-Remaining', (config.maxRequests - 1).toString());
        next();
      }
    } catch (err) {
      logger.error({ error: err, key }, 'Rate limit check error');
      // Fail open - don't block legitimate users on error
      next();
    }
  };
}

export const magicLinkRateLimit = () => rateLimit(magicLinkConfig);
export const apiRateLimit = () => rateLimit(defaultConfig);
```

### 📁 `packages/api/src/controllers/auth.controller.ts`

```typescript
import { Request, Response } from 'express';
import { createClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js';
import { z } from 'zod';
import pino from 'pino';
import { AuthRequest } from '../middleware/auth.js';
import { hashEmail } from '../utils/logger.js';

const logger = pino({ level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info' });

const supabase = createClient(
  process.env.SUPABASE_URL!,
  process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!
);

// Validation schemas
const magicLinkSchema = z.object({
  email: z.string().email('Invalid email format'),
  role: z.enum(['pilgrim', 'agency']),
});

/**
 * POST /api/v1/auth/magic-link
 * Send magic link to user's email
 */
export async function sendMagicLink(
  req: Request,
  res: Response
): Promise<void> {
  try {
    const validationResult = magicLinkSchema.safeParse(req.body);

    if (!validationResult.success) {
      logger.warn({ errors: validationResult.error.errors }, 'Invalid magic link request');
      res.status(400).json({
        error: {
          code: 'VALIDATION_ERROR',
          message: 'Invalid input',
          details: { field_errors: validationResult.error.errors },
        },
      });
      return;
    }

    const { email, role } = validationResult.data;

    // Check if user exists (don't reveal if account exists for security)
    const {  existingUser } = await supabase
      .from('users')
      .select('id, role')
      .eq('email', email.toLowerCase())
      .single();

    if (existingUser && existingUser.role !== role) {
      logger.warn({ emailHash: hashEmail(email) }, 'Role mismatch for magic link');
      // Still send link to avoid enumeration, but log discrepancy
    }

    // Send magic link via Supabase Auth
    const { error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithOtp({
      email: email.toLowerCase(),
    });

    if (error) {
      logger.error({ error: error.message, emailHash: hashEmail(email) }, 'Magic link send failed');
      res.status(500).json({
        error: {
          code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
          message: 'Failed to send magic link',
        },
      });
      return;
    }

    logger.info({ emailHash: hashEmail(email), role }, 'Magic link sent');

    // Don't reveal if account exists (security best practice)
    res.status(200).json({
      message: 'Magic link sent if account exists',
    });
  } catch (err) {
    logger.error({ error: err }, 'Send magic link error');
    res.status(500).json({
      error: {
        code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
        message: 'Unexpected error',
      },
    });
  }
}

/**
 * GET /api/v1/me
 * Get current authenticated user info
 */
export async function getCurrentUser(
  req: AuthRequest,
  res: Response
): Promise<void> {
  try {
    if (!req.user) {
      res.status(401).json({
        error: { code: 'UNAUTHORIZED', message: 'Not authenticated' },
      });
      return;
    }

    res.status(200).json({
      user: {
        id: req.user.id,
        agency_id: req.user.agency_id,
        role: req.user.role,
        email: req.user.email,
        meta req.user.metadata,
      },
    });
  } catch (err) {
    logger.error({ error: err }, 'Get current user error');
    res.status(500).json({
      error: {
        code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
        message: 'Failed to fetch user info',
      },
    });
  }
}

/**
 * POST /api/v1/auth/logout
 * Invalidate current session
 */
export async function logout(
  req: AuthRequest,
  res: Response
): Promise<void> {
  try {
    if (!req.user) {
      res.status(401).json({
        error: { code: 'UNAUTHORIZED', message: 'Not authenticated' },
      });
      return;
    }

    // Supabase handles token invalidation on client side
    logger.info({ userIdHash: hashEmail(req.user.email) }, 'User logged out');

    res.status(200).json({
      message: 'Logged out successfully',
    });
  } catch (err) {
    logger.error({ error: err }, 'Logout error');
    res.status(500).json({
      error: {
        code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
        message: 'Logout failed',
      },
    });
  }
}
```

### 📁 `packages/api/src/routes/auth.routes.ts`

```typescript
import { Router } from 'express';
import { sendMagicLink, getCurrentUser, logout } from '../controllers/auth.controller.js';
import { authMiddleware } from '../middleware/auth.js';
import { magicLinkRateLimit, apiRateLimit } from '../middleware/rate-limit.js';

const router = Router();

/**
 * @route POST /api/v1/auth/magic-link
 * @desc Send magic link for authentication
 * @access Public (rate limited)
 */
router.post('/magic-link', magicLinkRateLimit(), sendMagicLink);

/**
 * @route GET /api/v1/me
 * @desc Get current authenticated user
 * @access Private
 */
router.get('/me', apiRateLimit(), authMiddleware, getCurrentUser);

/**
 * @route POST /api/v1/auth/logout
 * @desc Logout current user
 * @access Private
 */
router.post('/logout', authMiddleware, logout);

export default router;
```

### 📁 `database/policies/rls_policies_complete.sql`

```sql
-- ===========================================
-- RLS Policies - Complete Implementation
-- For: Mon Omra MVP Lot 1
-- ===========================================

-- Enable RLS on all business tables
ALTER TABLE agencies ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE users ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE pilgrims ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE groups ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE flights ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE hotels ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE program_items ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE documents ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE payments ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE tickets ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE notifications ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

-- ===========================================
-- Agency Isolation Policies
-- Applied to all business tables
-- ===========================================

-- Pilgrims
CREATE POLICY agency_isolation_pilgrims ON pilgrims
  FOR ALL USING (agency_id = app.current_agency_id())
  WITH CHECK (agency_id = app.current_agency_id());

-- Groups
CREATE POLICY agency_isolation_groups ON groups
  FOR ALL USING (agency_id = app.current_agency_id())
  WITH CHECK (agency_id = app.current_agency_id());

-- Flights
CREATE POLICY agency_isolation_flights ON flights
  FOR ALL USING (agency_id = app.current_agency_id())
  WITH CHECK (agency_id = app.current_agency_id());

-- Hotels
CREATE POLICY agency_isolation_hotels ON hotels
  FOR ALL USING (agency_id = app.current_agency_id())
  WITH CHECK (agency_id = app.current_agency_id());

-- Documents
CREATE POLICY agency_isolation_documents ON documents
  FOR ALL USING (agency_id = app.current_agency_id())
  WITH CHECK (agency_id = app.current_agency_id());

-- Payments
CREATE POLICY agency_isolation_payments ON payments
  FOR ALL USING (agency_id = app.current_agency_id())
  WITH CHECK (agency_id = app.current_agency_id());

-- Tickets
CREATE POLICY agency_isolation_tickets ON tickets
  FOR ALL USING (agency_id = app.current_agency_id())
  WITH CHECK (agency_id = app.current_agency_id());

-- Notifications
CREATE POLICY agency_isolation_notifications ON notifications
  FOR ALL USING (agency_id = app.current_agency_id())
  WITH CHECK (agency_id = app.current_agency_id());

-- ===========================================
-- Pilgrim Self-View Exception
-- Pilgrims can only view their own record
-- ===========================================

CREATE POLICY pilgrim_self_view ON pilgrims
  FOR SELECT USING (
    id = NULLIF(current_setting('app.current_pilgrim_id', true), '')::UUID
  );

CREATE POLICY pilgrim_self_documents ON documents
  FOR SELECT USING (
    pilgrim_id = NULLIF(current_setting('app.current_pilgrim_id', true), '')::UUID
    AND (expires_at IS NULL OR expires_at > NOW())
  );

CREATE POLICY pilgrim_self_tickets ON tickets
  FOR ALL USING (
    pilgrim_id = NULLIF(current_setting('app.current_pilgrim_id', true), '')::UUID
  );

-- ===========================================
-- Document Retention Policy
-- Auto-expire documents after retention period
-- ===========================================

CREATE POLICY documents_retention ON documents
  FOR SELECT USING (
    expires_at IS NULL OR expires_at > NOW()
  );

-- ===========================================
-- Audit Log Policies
-- Document access logs (insert only)
-- ===========================================

ALTER TABLE document_access_logs ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

CREATE POLICY audit_log_insert ON document_access_logs
  FOR INSERT WITH CHECK (true);

CREATE POLICY audit_log_select ON document_access_logs
  FOR SELECT USING (
    accessed_by_user_id = NULLIF(current_setting('app.current_user_id', true), '')::UUID
  );

-- ===========================================
-- Analytics Events Policy
-- Agency can view their own analytics
-- ===========================================

ALTER TABLE analytics_events ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

CREATE POLICY analytics_agency_view ON analytics_events
  FOR ALL USING (agency_id = app.current_agency_id());
```

### 📁 `packages/api/tests/auth.test.ts`

```typescript
import { describe, it, expect, beforeAll, afterAll } from 'vitest';
import request from 'supertest';
import { app } from '../src/app.js';
import { supabase } from './utils/supabase-test.js';

describe('Auth Module', () => {
  const testEmail = 'test.pilgrim@monomra-test.local';
  const testAgencyId = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000001';

  describe('POST /api/v1/auth/magic-link', () => {
    it('should accept valid email and role', async () => {
      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/v1/auth/magic-link')
        .send({ email: testEmail, role: 'pilgrim' });

      expect(response.status).toBe(200);
      expect(response.body.message).toContain('Magic link sent');
    });

    it('should reject invalid email format', async () => {
      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/v1/auth/magic-link')
        .send({ email: 'invalid-email', role: 'pilgrim' });

      expect(response.status).toBe(400);
      expect(response.body.error.code).toBe('VALIDATION_ERROR');
    });

    it('should rate limit after 5 requests per minute', async () => {
      for (let i = 0; i < 5; i++) {
        await request(app)
          .post('/api/v1/auth/magic-link')
          .send({ email: `ratelimit${i}@test.local`, role: 'pilgrim' });
      }

      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/v1/auth/magic-link')
        .send({ email: 'ratelimit6@test.local', role: 'pilgrim' });

      expect(response.status).toBe(429);
      expect(response.body.error.code).toBe('RATE_LIMITED');
    });
  });

  describe('GET /api/v1/me', () => {
    it('should return 401 without token', async () => {
      const response = await request(app).get('/api/v1/me');
      expect(response.status).toBe(401);
      expect(response.body.error.code).toBe('UNAUTHORIZED');
    });

    it('should return user info with valid token', async () => {
      // First get a token (mocked in test environment)
      const token = await getTestUserToken(testEmail);

      const response = await request(app)
        .get('/api/v1/me')
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${token}`);

      expect(response.status).toBe(200);
      expect(response.body.user.email).toBe(testEmail);
      expect(response.body.user.agency_id).toBe(testAgencyId);
    });
  });

  describe('RLS Isolation', () => {
    it('should prevent cross-agency access', async () => {
      const agencyAToken = await getTestUserToken('pilgrim@agency-a.local');
      const pilgrimFromAgencyB = 'pilgrim@agency-b.local';

      const response = await request(app)
        .get(`/api/v1/pilgrims/${pilgrimFromAgencyB}`)
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${agencyAToken}`);

      expect(response.status).toBe(403);
      expect(response.body.error.code).toBe('FORBIDDEN');
    });
  });
});

// Helper function for test token
async function getTestUserToken(email: string): Promise<string> {
  // In test environment, use Supabase test credentials
  const { data } = await supabase.auth.signInWithOtp({ email });
  return data?.session?.access_token || '';
}
```

## 1) NOVA-LEAD — Résumé & Décisions (Decision Log — Delta)

| Décision | Justification | Alternatives écartées | Impact | Version |
|----------|--------------|----------------------|--------|---------|
| **Storage : S3 SSE-S3 + pré-signed URLs 15min** | Conformité DPIA + sécurité accès temporaire | Proxy backend (complexité) / URLs permanentes (risque) | URLs expirant automatiquement, audit obligatoire | v1.7 |
| **Audit logs : écriture automatique sur chaque accès** | Traçabilité RGPD Art. 30 + DPIA | Logs applicatifs uniquement (moins fiable) | Table `document_access_logs` peuplée systématiquement | v1.7 |
| **Rétention : job quotidien + expiration DB** | Conformité durée conservation (24 mois) | Suppression manuelle (erreur humaine) | Champ `expires_at` + cron job automatique | v1.7 |
| **Types documents : whitelist stricte** | Sécurité + validation DPIA | Types libres (risque contenu malveillant) | enum PostgreSQL + validation Zod côté API | v1.7 |

| Élément | Mise à jour |
|---------|-------------|
| **Documents** | ✅ Types : passport, visa, ticket, contract, other • Stockage : S3 SSE-S3 • Accès : pré-signed URLs 15min • Audit : table `document_access_logs` • Rétention : 24 mois post-voyage |
| **Sécurité** | ✅ Chiffrement au repos (SSE-S3) + transit (TLS 1.3) • Whitelist content-type (PDF, JPEG, PNG) • Scan antivirus (P1) |
| **RGPD** | ✅ Audit logs obligatoires • DSAR inclut documents • Suppression auto après expiration |

export type DocumentType = 'passport' | 'visa' | 'ticket' | 'contract' | 'other';

export type DocumentContentType = 
  | 'application/pdf' 
  | 'image/jpeg' 
  | 'image/png';

export interface Document {
  id: string;
  agency_id: string;
  pilgrim_id: string;
  type: DocumentType;
  storage_key: string;
  filename: string;
  content_type: DocumentContentType;
  size_bytes: number;
  expires_at?: string;
  uploaded_at: string;
  uploaded_by_user_id: string;
}

export interface DocumentSummary {
  id: string;
  type: DocumentType;
  filename: string;
  uploaded_at: string;
  expires_at?: string;
}

export interface UploadUrlRequest {
  pilgrim_id: string;
  type: DocumentType;
  filename: string;
  content_type: DocumentContentType;
}

export interface UploadUrlResponse {
  upload_url: string;
  document_id: string;
  expires_in_sec: number;
}

export interface DownloadUrlResponse {
  download_url: string;
  expires_in_sec: number;
  filename: string;
}

export const DOCUMENT_RETENTION_MONTHS = 24;
export const URL_EXPIRY_SECONDS = 900; // 15 minutes

export const ALLOWED_CONTENT_TYPES: DocumentContentType[] = [
  'application/pdf',
  'image/jpeg',
  'image/png',
];

export const MAX_FILE_SIZE_BYTES = 10 * 1024 * 1024; // 10MB

### 📁 `packages/api/src/services/storage.service.ts`

```typescript
import { S3Client, PutObjectCommand, GetObjectCommand, DeleteObjectCommand } from '@aws-sdk/client-s3';
import { getSignedUrl } from '@aws-sdk/s3-request-presigner';
import pino from 'pino';

const logger = pino({ level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info' });

const s3Client = new S3Client({
  region: process.env.S3_REGION || 'eu-west-3',
  endpoint: process.env.S3_ENDPOINT,
  credentials: {
    accessKeyId: process.env.S3_ACCESS_KEY!,
    secretAccessKey: process.env.S3_SECRET_KEY!,
  },
  forcePathStyle: true, // Required for R2 compatibility
});

const BUCKET_NAME = process.env.S3_BUCKET!;

/**
 * Generate S3 object key with agency/pilgrim prefix
 * Ensures logical isolation even at storage level
 */
function generateObjectKey(agencyId: string, pilgrimId: string, documentId: string, filename: string): string {
  const sanitizedFilename = filename.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9.-]/g, '_');
  return `agencies/${agencyId}/pilgrims/${pilgrimId}/documents/${documentId}/${sanitizedFilename}`;
}

/**
 * Generate pre-signed upload URL
 */
export async function generateUploadUrl(
  objectKey: string,
  contentType: string,
  expirySeconds: number = 900
): Promise<string> {
  const command = new PutObjectCommand({
    Bucket: BUCKET_NAME,
    Key: objectKey,
    ContentType: contentType,
    ServerSideEncryption: 'AES256', // SSE-S3 encryption
  });

  const url = await getSignedUrl(s3Client, command, { expiresIn: expirySeconds });
  
  logger.info({ objectKey, expirySeconds }, 'Upload URL generated');
  
  return url;
}

/**
 * Generate pre-signed download URL
 */
export async function generateDownloadUrl(
  objectKey: string,
  filename: string,
  expirySeconds: number = 900
): Promise<string> {
  const command = new GetObjectCommand({
    Bucket: BUCKET_NAME,
    Key: objectKey,
    ResponseContentDisposition: `attachment; filename="${filename}"`,
  });

  const url = await getSignedUrl(s3Client, command, { expiresIn: expirySeconds });
  
  logger.info({ objectKey, expirySeconds }, 'Download URL generated');
  
  return url;
}

/**
 * Delete document from storage
 */
export async function deleteDocument(objectKey: string): Promise<void> {
  try {
    const command = new DeleteObjectCommand({
      Bucket: BUCKET_NAME,
      Key: objectKey,
    });

    await s3Client.send(command);
    
    logger.info({ objectKey }, 'Document deleted from storage');
  } catch (err) {
    logger.error({ error: err, objectKey }, 'Failed to delete document');
    throw err;
  }
}

/**
 * Verify object exists (for validation)
 */
export async function objectExists(objectKey: string): Promise<boolean> {
  try {
    const command = new GetObjectCommand({
      Bucket: BUCKET_NAME,
      Key: objectKey,
    });

    await s3Client.send(command);
    return true;
  } catch (err) {
    return false;
  }
}
```

---

### 📁 `packages/api/src/controllers/documents.controller.ts`

```typescript
import { Response } from 'express';
import { z } from 'zod';
import pino from 'pino';
import { createClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js';
import { AuthRequest } from '../middleware/auth.js';
import { generateUploadUrl, generateDownloadUrl, deleteDocument } from '../services/storage.service.js';
import { 
  DOCUMENT_RETENTION_MONTHS, 
  URL_EXPIRY_SECONDS, 
  ALLOWED_CONTENT_TYPES,
  MAX_FILE_SIZE_BYTES 
} from '@mon-omra/shared';
import { hashEmail } from '../utils/logger.js';

const logger = pino({ level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info' });

const supabase = createClient(
  process.env.SUPABASE_URL!,
  process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!
);

// Validation schemas
const uploadUrlSchema = z.object({
  pilgrim_id: z.string().uuid('Invalid pilgrim ID'),
  type: z.enum(['passport', 'visa', 'ticket', 'contract', 'other']),
  filename: z.string().min(1).max(255),
  content_type: z.enum(ALLOWED_CONTENT_TYPES),
});

/**
 * POST /api/v1/documents/upload-url
 * Generate pre-signed upload URL for document
 */
export async function getUploadUrl(
  req: AuthRequest,
  res: Response
): Promise<void> {
  try {
    if (!req.user || !req.agency_id) {
      res.status(401).json({
        error: { code: 'UNAUTHORIZED', message: 'Authentication required' },
      });
      return;
    }

    // Only agency roles can upload documents
    if (!['super_admin', 'ops'].includes(req.user.role)) {
      res.status(403).json({
        error: { code: 'FORBIDDEN', message: 'Only agency staff can upload documents' },
      });
      return;
    }

    const validationResult = uploadUrlSchema.safeParse(req.body);

    if (!validationResult.success) {
      logger.warn({ errors: validationResult.error.errors }, 'Invalid upload URL request');
      res.status(400).json({
        error: {
          code: 'VALIDATION_ERROR',
          message: 'Invalid input',
          details: { field_errors: validationResult.error.errors },
        },
      });
      return;
    }

    const { pilgrim_id, type, filename, content_type } = validationResult.data;

    // Verify pilgrim belongs to user's agency (anti-IDOR)
    const {  pilgrim } = await supabase
      .from('pilgrims')
      .select('id, agency_id')
      .eq('id', pilgrim_id)
      .eq('agency_id', req.agency_id)
      .single();

    if (!pilgrim) {
      logger.warn({ pilgrim_id, agency_id: req.agency_id }, 'Pilgrim not found or access denied');
      res.status(403).json({
        error: { code: 'FORBIDDEN', message: 'Cannot upload for this pilgrim' },
      });
      return;
    }

    // Calculate expiration date (24 months from now)
    const expiresAt = new Date();
    expiresAt.setMonth(expiresAt.getMonth() + DOCUMENT_RETENTION_MONTHS);

    // Create document record in database
    const documentId = crypto.randomUUID();
    const storageKey = `agencies/${req.agency_id}/pilgrims/${pilgrim_id}/documents/${documentId}/${filename}`;

    const {  documentRecord, error: dbError } = await supabase
      .from('documents')
      .insert({
        id: documentId,
        agency_id: req.agency_id,
        pilgrim_id,
        type,
        storage_key: storageKey,
        filename,
        content_type,
        expires_at: expiresAt.toISOString(),
        uploaded_by_user_id: req.user.id,
      })
      .select()
      .single();

    if (dbError || !documentRecord) {
      logger.error({ error: dbError }, 'Failed to create document record');
      res.status(500).json({
        error: {
          code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
          message: 'Failed to create document record',
        },
      });
      return;
    }

    // Generate pre-signed upload URL
    const uploadUrl = await generateUploadUrl(storageKey, content_type, URL_EXPIRY_SECONDS);

    logger.info({
      documentId,
      pilgrimId: pilgrim_id,
      type,
      userIdHash: hashEmail(req.user.email),
    }, 'Document upload URL generated');

    res.status(200).json({
      upload_url: uploadUrl,
      document_id: documentId,
      expires_in_sec: URL_EXPIRY_SECONDS,
    });
  } catch (err) {
    logger.error({ error: err }, 'Get upload URL error');
    res.status(500).json({
      error: {
        code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
        message: 'Failed to generate upload URL',
      },
    });
  }
}

/**
 * GET /api/v1/documents/:id/download-url
 * Generate pre-signed download URL for document
 */
export async function getDownloadUrl(
  req: AuthRequest,
  res: Response
): Promise<void> {
  try {
    if (!req.user || !req.agency_id) {
      res.status(401).json({
        error: { code: 'UNAUTHORIZED', message: 'Authentication required' },
      });
      return;
    }

    const documentId = req.params.id;

    // Fetch document with agency check
    const {  document } = await supabase
      .from('documents')
      .select('id, agency_id, pilgrim_id, storage_key, filename, expires_at, type')
      .eq('id', documentId)
      .single();

    if (!document) {
      logger.warn({ documentId }, 'Document not found');
      res.status(404).json({
        error: { code: 'NOT_FOUND', message: 'Document not found' },
      });
      return;
    }

    // Check expiration
    if (document.expires_at && new Date(document.expires_at) < new Date()) {
      logger.warn({ documentId, expiresAt: document.expires_at }, 'Document expired');
      res.status(410).json({
        error: { code: 'EXPIRED', message: 'Document retention period exceeded' },
      });
      return;
    }

    // Check access permissions
    const isAgencyStaff = ['super_admin', 'ops', 'support'].includes(req.user.role);
    const isPilgrimSelf = req.user.role === 'pilgrim' && document.pilgrim_id === req.user.id;

    if (!isAgencyStaff && !isPilgrimSelf) {
      logger.warn({
        documentId,
        userIdHash: hashEmail(req.user.email),
        userRole: req.user.role,
      }, 'Document access denied');
      res.status(403).json({
        error: { code: 'FORBIDDEN', message: 'Access denied to this document' },
      });
      return;
    }

    // Generate pre-signed download URL
    const downloadUrl = await generateDownloadUrl(
      document.storage_key,
      document.filename,
      URL_EXPIRY_SECONDS
    );

    // Log access for audit (RGPD requirement)
    await supabase
      .from('document_access_logs')
      .insert({
        document_id: documentId,
        accessed_by_user_id: req.user.id,
        ip_address: req.ip || req.socket.remoteAddress,
        user_agent: req.headers['user-agent'],
      });

    logger.info({
      documentId,
      type: document.type,
      userIdHash: hashEmail(req.user.email),
      userRole: req.user.role,
    }, 'Document download URL generated');

    res.status(200).json({
      download_url: downloadUrl,
      expires_in_sec: URL_EXPIRY_SECONDS,
      filename: document.filename,
    });
  } catch (err) {
    logger.error({ error: err }, 'Get download URL error');
    res.status(500).json({
      error: {
        code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
        message: 'Failed to generate download URL',
      },
    });
  }
}

/**
 * GET /api/v1/pilgrims/:pilgrimId/documents
 * List documents for a pilgrim
 */
export async function listPilgrimDocuments(
  req: AuthRequest,
  res: Response
): Promise<void> {
  try {
    if (!req.user || !req.agency_id) {
      res.status(401).json({
        error: { code: 'UNAUTHORIZED', message: 'Authentication required' },
      });
      return;
    }

    const pilgrimId = req.params.pilgrimId;

    // Verify pilgrim belongs to user's agency or is self
    const isPilgrimSelf = req.user.role === 'pilgrim' && pilgrimId === req.user.id;

    if (!isPilgrimSelf) {
      const {  pilgrim } = await supabase
        .from('pilgrims')
        .select('id, agency_id')
        .eq('id', pilgrimId)
        .eq('agency_id', req.agency_id)
        .single();

      if (!pilgrim) {
        res.status(403).json({
          error: { code: 'FORBIDDEN', message: 'Access denied to this pilgrim' },
        });
        return;
      }
    }

    // Fetch documents (not expired)
    const {  documents } = await supabase
      .from('documents')
      .select('id, type, filename, uploaded_at, expires_at')
      .eq('pilgrim_id', pilgrimId)
      .eq('agency_id', req.agency_id)
      .or(`expires_at.is.null,expires_at.gt.${new Date().toISOString()}`)
      .order('uploaded_at', { ascending: false });

    res.status(200).json({
      documents: documents || [],
    });
  } catch (err) {
    logger.error({ error: err }, 'List documents error');
    res.status(500).json({
      error: {
        code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
        message: 'Failed to list documents',
      },
    });
  }
}

/**
 * DELETE /api/v1/documents/:id
 * Delete document (soft delete + schedule storage deletion)
 */
export async function deleteDocument(
  req: AuthRequest,
  res: Response
): Promise<void> {
  try {
    if (!req.user || !req.agency_id) {
      res.status(401).json({
        error: { code: 'UNAUTHORIZED', message: 'Authentication required' },
      });
      return;
    }

    // Only ops and super_admin can delete
    if (!['super_admin', 'ops'].includes(req.user.role)) {
      res.status(403).json({
        error: { code: 'FORBIDDEN', message: 'Insufficient permissions to delete' },
      });
      return;
    }

    const documentId = req.params.id;

    // Fetch document
    const {  document } = await supabase
      .from('documents')
      .select('id, agency_id, storage_key')
      .eq('id', documentId)
      .single();

    if (!document) {
      res.status(404).json({
        error: { code: 'NOT_FOUND', message: 'Document not found' },
      });
      return;
    }

    // Verify agency
    if (document.agency_id !== req.agency_id) {
      res.status(403).json({
        error: { code: 'FORBIDDEN', message: 'Access denied' },
      });
      return;
    }

    // Delete from storage
    await deleteDocument(document.storage_key);

    // Delete from database
    await supabase
      .from('documents')
      .delete()
      .eq('id', documentId);

    logger.info({
      documentId,
      userIdHash: hashEmail(req.user.email),
    }, 'Document deleted');

    res.status(200).json({
      message: 'Document deleted successfully',
    });
  } catch (err) {
    logger.error({ error: err }, 'Delete document error');
    res.status(500).json({
      error: {
        code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
        message: 'Failed to delete document',
      },
    });
  }
}
```

### 📁 `packages/api/src/jobs/document-retention.job.ts`

```typescript
import { createClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js';
import pino from 'pino';
import { deleteDocument } from '../services/storage.service.js';

const logger = pino({ level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info' });

const supabase = createClient(
  process.env.SUPABASE_URL!,
  process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!
);

/**
 * Daily job to purge expired documents
 * Runs automatically via cron scheduler
 */
export async function runDocumentRetentionPurge(): Promise<{
  purged: number;
  errors: number;
}> {
  const result = { purged: 0, errors: 0 };

  try {
    logger.info('Starting document retention purge job');

    // Fetch expired documents
    const {  expiredDocuments } = await supabase
      .from('documents')
      .select('id, storage_key, pilgrim_id, type')
      .lt('expires_at', new Date().toISOString())
      .limit(100); // Batch processing

    if (!expiredDocuments || expiredDocuments.length === 0) {
      logger.info('No expired documents to purge');
      return result;
    }

    logger.info({ count: expiredDocuments.length }, 'Found expired documents');

    // Process each document
    for (const doc of expiredDocuments) {
      try {
        // Delete from storage
        await deleteDocument(doc.storage_key);

        // Delete from database
        await supabase
          .from('documents')
          .delete()
          .eq('id', doc.id);

        result.purged++;

        logger.info({
          documentId: doc.id,
          pilgrimId: doc.pilgrim_id,
          type: doc.type,
        }, 'Expired document purged');
      } catch (err) {
        result.errors++;
        logger.error({
          error: err,
          documentId: doc.id,
        }, 'Failed to purge expired document');
      }
    }

    logger.info({
      purged: result.purged,
      errors: result.errors,
    }, 'Document retention purge completed');

    return result;
  } catch (err) {
    logger.error({ error: err }, 'Document retention purge job failed');
    throw err;
  }
}

// Schedule: Run daily at 2 AM UTC
// In production, use a cron service (e.g., GitHub Actions, AWS EventBridge, etc.)
```

### 📁 `packages/api/src/routes/documents.routes.ts`

```typescript
import { Router } from 'express';
import {
  getUploadUrl,
  getDownloadUrl,
  listPilgrimDocuments,
  deleteDocument,
} from '../controllers/documents.controller.js';
import { authMiddleware, requireRoles } from '../middleware/auth.js';
import { apiRateLimit } from '../middleware/rate-limit.js';

const router = Router();

// All document routes require authentication
router.use(authMiddleware);
router.use(apiRateLimit());

/**
 * @route POST /api/v1/documents/upload-url
 * @desc Generate pre-signed upload URL
 * @access Agency (super_admin, ops only)
 */
router.post('/upload-url', requireRoles('super_admin', 'ops'), getUploadUrl);

/**
 * @route GET /api/v1/documents/:id/download-url
 * @desc Generate pre-signed download URL
 * @access Agency staff or pilgrim self
 */
router.get('/:id/download-url', getDownloadUrl);

/**
 * @route GET /api/v1/pilgrims/:pilgrimId/documents
 * @desc List all documents for a pilgrim
 * @access Agency staff or pilgrim self
 */
router.get('/pilgrims/:pilgrimId/documents', listPilgrimDocuments);

/**
 * @route DELETE /api/v1/documents/:id
 * @desc Delete a document
 * @access Agency (super_admin, ops only)
 */
router.delete('/:id', requireRoles('super_admin', 'ops'), deleteDocument);

export default router;
```

### 📁 `database/migrations/004_create_documents_tables.sql`

```sql
-- ===========================================
-- Documents Module Tables
-- Mon Omra MVP Lot 1
-- ===========================================

-- Documents table
CREATE TABLE documents (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  agency_id UUID NOT NULL,
  pilgrim_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES pilgrims(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  type TEXT CHECK (type IN ('passport', 'visa', 'ticket', 'contract', 'other')),
  storage_key TEXT NOT NULL,
  filename TEXT NOT NULL,
  content_type TEXT CHECK (content_type IN ('application/pdf', 'image/jpeg', 'image/png')),
  size_bytes INTEGER,
  expires_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  uploaded_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  uploaded_by_user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id)
);

-- Document access logs (audit trail for RGPD)
CREATE TABLE document_access_logs (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  document_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES documents(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  accessed_by_user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  accessed_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  ip_address INET,
  user_agent TEXT
);

-- Indexes for performance
CREATE INDEX idx_documents_agency_pilgrim ON documents(agency_id, pilgrim_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_documents_expires_at ON documents(expires_at);
CREATE INDEX idx_documents_pilgrim_type ON documents(pilgrim_id, type);
CREATE INDEX idx_access_logs_document ON document_access_logs(document_id, accessed_at);
CREATE INDEX idx_access_logs_user ON document_access_logs(accessed_by_user_id, accessed_at);

-- RLS policies are in: database/policies/rls_policies_complete.sql
```

### 📁 `packages/api/tests/documents.test.ts`

```typescript
import { describe, it, expect, beforeAll } from 'vitest';
import request from 'supertest';
import { app } from '../src/app.js';
import { supabase } from './utils/supabase-test.js';

describe('Documents Module', () => {
  let agencyToken: string;
  let pilgrimToken: string;
  let pilgrimId: string;
  let documentId: string;

  beforeAll(async () => {
    agencyToken = await getTestUserToken('ops@agency-a.local');
    pilgrimToken = await getTestUserToken('pilgrim@agency-a.local');
    
    // Get pilgrim ID
    const {  user } = await supabase
      .from('users')
      .select('id')
      .eq('email', 'pilgrim@agency-a.local')
      .single();
    pilgrimId = user.id;
  });

  describe('POST /api/v1/documents/upload-url', () => {
    it('should generate upload URL for agency ops role', async () => {
      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/v1/documents/upload-url')
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${agencyToken}`)
        .send({
          pilgrim_id: pilgrimId,
          type: 'visa',
          filename: 'visa.pdf',
          content_type: 'application/pdf',
        });

      expect(response.status).toBe(200);
      expect(response.body.upload_url).toContain('X-Amz-Signature');
      expect(response.body.expires_in_sec).toBe(900);
      documentId = response.body.document_id;
    });

    it('should reject pilgrim role from uploading', async () => {
      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/v1/documents/upload-url')
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${pilgrimToken}`)
        .send({
          pilgrim_id: pilgrimId,
          type: 'visa',
          filename: 'visa.pdf',
          content_type: 'application/pdf',
        });

      expect(response.status).toBe(403);
      expect(response.body.error.code).toBe('FORBIDDEN');
    });

    it('should reject cross-agency upload attempt', async () => {
      const otherAgencyToken = await getTestUserToken('ops@agency-b.local');
      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/v1/documents/upload-url')
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${otherAgencyToken}`)
        .send({
          pilgrim_id: pilgrimId,
          type: 'visa',
          filename: 'visa.pdf',
          content_type: 'application/pdf',
        });

      expect(response.status).toBe(403);
      expect(response.body.error.code).toBe('FORBIDDEN');
    });
  });

  describe('GET /api/v1/documents/:id/download-url', () => {
    it('should generate download URL for authorized user', async () => {
      const response = await request(app)
        .get(`/api/v1/documents/${documentId}/download-url`)
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${agencyToken}`);

      expect(response.status).toBe(200);
      expect(response.body.download_url).toContain('X-Amz-Signature');
    });

    it('should allow pilgrim to download own document', async () => {
      const response = await request(app)
        .get(`/api/v1/documents/${documentId}/download-url`)
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${pilgrimToken}`);

      expect(response.status).toBe(200);
    });

    it('should reject cross-agency download attempt', async () => {
      const otherAgencyToken = await getTestUserToken('ops@agency-b.local');
      const response = await request(app)
        .get(`/api/v1/documents/${documentId}/download-url`)
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${otherAgencyToken}`);

      expect(response.status).toBe(403);
      expect(response.body.error.code).toBe('FORBIDDEN');
    });
  });

  describe('GET /api/v1/pilgrims/:pilgrimId/documents', () => {
    it('should list documents for authorized pilgrim', async () => {
      const response = await request(app)
        .get(`/api/v1/pilgrims/${pilgrimId}/documents`)
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${agencyToken}`);

      expect(response.status).toBe(200);
      expect(Array.isArray(response.body.documents)).toBe(true);
    });
  });
});

async function getTestUserToken(email: string): Promise<string> {
  const { data } = await supabase.auth.signInWithOtp({ email });
  return data?.session?.access_token || '';
}
```

### 📁 `packages/web/app/dashboard/page.tsx`

```typescript
'use client';

import { useAuth } from '@/lib/auth';
import { usePilgrimDashboard } from '@/hooks/usePilgrimDashboard';
import { DashboardSkeleton } from './components/DashboardSkeleton';
import { TripHeader } from './components/TripHeader';
import { NextActionCard } from './components/NextActionCard';
import { PaymentStatusCard } from './components/PaymentStatusCard';
import { DocumentGrid } from './components/DocumentGrid';
import { QuickActions } from './components/QuickActions';
import { ErrorBoundary } from '@/components/ErrorBoundary';
import { useEffect } from 'react';
import { trackEvent } from '@/lib/analytics';

export default function DashboardPage() {
  const { user, isLoading: authLoading } = useAuth();
  const { data, isLoading, error, refetch } = usePilgrimDashboard();

  // Track dashboard view (analytics)
  useEffect(() => {
    if (data && !isLoading) {
      trackEvent('dashboard_viewed', {
        pilgrim_id: user?.id,
        departure_date: data.group?.departure_date,
      });
    }
  }, [data, isLoading, user?.id]);

  // Loading state
  if (authLoading || isLoading) {
    return <DashboardSkeleton />;
  }

  // Error state
  if (error) {
    return (
      <ErrorBoundary
        error={error}
        onRetry={() => refetch()}
        title="Impossible de charger votre dossier"
        message="Vérifiez votre connexion et réessayez."
      />
    );
  }

  // Empty state (no trip data)
  if (!data || !data.pilgrim) {
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center p-4">
        <div className="text-center max-w-md">
          <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900 mb-2">
            Aucun voyage trouvé
          </h1>
          <p className="text-gray-600 mb-4">
            Votre agence n'a pas encore publié les détails de votre voyage.
          </p>
          <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">
            Contactez votre agence pour plus d'informations.
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <ErrorBoundary>
      <main className="min-h-screen bg-gray-50 pb-20">
        {/* Header with user info */}
        <header className="bg-white border-b border-gray-200 sticky top-0 z-10">
          <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto px-4 py-3 flex items-center justify-between">
            <div>
              <h1 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900">
                Mon Omra
              </h1>
              <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">
                {data.pilgrim.first_name} {data.pilgrim.last_name}
              </p>
            </div>
            <QuickActions />
          </div>
        </header>

        {/* Main content */}
        <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto px-4 py-6 space-y-6">
          {/* Trip Summary - Priority 1 */}
          <TripHeader
            departureDate={data.group?.departure_date}
            flight={data.flights[0]}
            destination={data.group?.city}
          />

          {/* Next Action - Priority 2 */}
          {data.next_action && (
            <NextActionCard action={data.next_action} />
          )}

          {/* Payment Status - Priority 3 */}
          <PaymentStatusCard payment={data.payment_status} />

          {/* Documents - Priority 4 */}
          <DocumentGrid documents={data.documents} />
        </div>
      </main>
    </ErrorBoundary>
  );
}
```

### 📁 `packages/web/app/dashboard/components/TripHeader.tsx`

```typescript
'use client';

import { FlightSummary } from '@mon-omra/shared';
import { PlaneIcon, CalendarIcon, MapPinIcon } from '@/components/icons';

interface TripHeaderProps {
  departureDate?: string;
  flight?: FlightSummary;
  destination?: string;
}

export function TripHeader({ departureDate, flight, destination }: TripHeaderProps) {
  const formatDate = (dateString?: string) => {
    if (!dateString) return 'Non défini';
    return new Date(dateString).toLocaleDateString('fr-FR', {
      weekday: 'long',
      year: 'numeric',
      month: 'long',
      day: 'numeric',
    });
  };

  return (
    <section 
      className="bg-gradient-to-r from-emerald-600 to-teal-600 rounded-2xl p-6 text-white shadow-lg"
      aria-label="Résumé du voyage"
    >
      {/* Departure Date */}
      <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-4">
        <CalendarIcon className="w-5 h-5" />
        <span className="text-sm font-medium opacity-90">
          Départ : {formatDate(departureDate)}
        </span>
      </div>

      {/* Flight Info */}
      {flight && (
        <div className="space-y-4">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
            <div className="bg-white/20 rounded-full p-2">
              <PlaneIcon className="w-6 h-6" />
            </div>
            <div>
              <p className="text-sm opacity-90">Vol principal</p>
              <p className="text-xl font-bold">{flight.flight_number}</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Route */}
          <div className="bg-white/10 rounded-xl p-4">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
              <div className="text-center">
                <p className="text-2xl font-bold">CDG</p>
                <p className="text-xs opacity-80">Paris</p>
              </div>
              
              <div className="flex-1 px-4">
                <div className="border-t-2 border-dashed border-white/50 relative">
                  <div className="absolute top-1/2 left-1/2 transform -translate-x-1/2 -translate-y-1/2">
                    <PlaneIcon className="w-4 h-4 text-white" />
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
              
              <div className="text-center">
                <p className="text-2xl font-bold">MED</p>
                <p className="text-xs opacity-80">Médine</p>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Flight Times */}
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4 text-sm">
            <div>
              <p className="opacity-80">Départ</p>
              <p className="font-semibold">
                {new Date(flight.departure_at).toLocaleTimeString('fr-FR', {
                  hour: '2-digit',
                  minute: '2-digit',
                })}
              </p>
            </div>
            <div>
              <p className="opacity-80">Arrivée</p>
              <p className="font-semibold">
                {new Date(flight.arrival_at).toLocaleTimeString('fr-FR', {
                  hour: '2-digit',
                  minute: '2-digit',
                })}
              </p>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Baggage Info */}
          {flight.baggage_policy && (
            <div className="bg-white/10 rounded-lg p-3 text-sm">
              <p className="opacity-80">Bagages inclus</p>
              <p className="font-semibold">
                {flight.baggage_policy.included} valise(s) de {flight.baggage_policy.weight_kg}kg
              </p>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      )}

      {!flight && (
        <div className="bg-white/10 rounded-lg p-4 text-center">
          <p className="text-sm">
            Les informations de vol seront publiées prochainement.
          </p>
        </div>
      )}
    </section>
  );
}

### 📁 `packages/web/app/dashboard/components/NextActionCard.tsx`

```typescript
'use client';

import { ActionItem } from '@mon-omra/shared';
import { AlertCircleIcon, CheckCircleIcon, ClockIcon } from '@/components/icons';
import Link from 'next/link';

interface NextActionCardProps {
  action: ActionItem;
}

export function NextActionCard({ action }: NextActionCardProps) {
  const getPriorityColor = (type: ActionItem['type']) => {
    switch (type) {
      case 'visa':
        return 'bg-red-50 border-red-200 text-red-900';
      case 'payment':
        return 'bg-orange-50 border-orange-200 text-orange-900';
      case 'document':
        return 'bg-blue-50 border-blue-200 text-blue-900';
      case 'checkin':
        return 'bg-emerald-50 border-emerald-200 text-emerald-900';
      default:
        return 'bg-gray-50 border-gray-200 text-gray-900';
    }
  };

  const getIcon = () => {
    if (action.completed) {
      return <CheckCircleIcon className="w-6 h-6 text-emerald-600" />;
    }
    
    switch (action.type) {
      case 'visa':
      case 'document':
        return <AlertCircleIcon className="w-6 h-6" />;
      case 'checkin':
        return <ClockIcon className="w-6 h-6" />;
      default:
        return <AlertCircleIcon className="w-6 h-6" />;
    }
  };

  const formatDueDate = (dateString?: string) => {
    if (!dateString) return null;
    const dueDate = new Date(dateString);
    const now = new Date();
    const daysLeft = Math.ceil((dueDate.getTime() - now.getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
    
    if (daysLeft < 0) return 'En retard';
    if (daysLeft === 0) return "Pour aujourd'hui";
    if (daysLeft === 1) return 'Pour demain';
    return `Dans ${daysLeft} jours`;
  };

  return (
    <section
      className={`rounded-xl border-2 p-4 ${getPriorityColor(action.type)}`}
      aria-label="Prochaine étape importante"
    >
      <div className="flex items-start gap-3">
        <div className="flex-shrink-0">
          {getIcon()}
        </div>
        
        <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
          <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-1">
            {action.label}
          </h2>
          
          {action.due_date && (
            <p className="text-sm opacity-80 mb-3">
              {formatDueDate(action.due_date)}
            </p>
          )}
          
          {action.completed ? (
            <span className="inline-flex items-center text-sm font-medium text-emerald-700">
              <CheckCircleIcon className="w-4 h-4 mr-1" />
              Terminé
            </span>
          ) : (
            <Link
              href={getActionLink(action.type)}
              className="inline-flex items-center justify-center px-4 py-2 bg-white border border-current rounded-lg text-sm font-medium hover:bg-opacity-90 transition-colors focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-offset-2 focus:ring-current"
            >
              Voir les détails
            </Link>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>
  );
}

function getActionLink(type: ActionItem['type']): string {
  switch (type) {
    case 'checkin':
      return '/dashboard/checkin';
    case 'payment':
      return '/dashboard/payment';
    case 'document':
      return '/dashboard/documents';
    case 'visa':
      return '/dashboard/visa';
    default:
      return '/dashboard';
  }
}
```

### 📁 `packages/web/app/dashboard/components/PaymentStatusCard.tsx`

```typescript
'use client';

import { PaymentStatus } from '@mon-omra/shared';
import { EuroIcon, CheckCircleIcon, AlertCircleIcon } from '@/components/icons';

interface PaymentStatusCardProps {
  payment: PaymentStatus;
}

export function PaymentStatusCard({ payment }: PaymentStatusCardProps) {
  const formatAmount = (cents: number) => {
    return new Intl.NumberFormat('fr-FR', {
      style: 'currency',
      currency: payment.currency || 'EUR',
    }).format(cents / 100);
  };

  const getProgressPercentage = () => {
    if (payment.total_amount_cents === 0) return 0;
    return (payment.paid_amount_cents / payment.total_amount_cents) * 100;
  };

  const getStatusConfig = () => {
    switch (payment.status) {
      case 'paid':
        return {
          color: 'bg-emerald-50 border-emerald-200',
          icon: <CheckCircleIcon className="w-6 h-6 text-emerald-600" />,
          label: 'Payé',
          textColor: 'text-emerald-900',
        };
      case 'partial':
        return {
          color: 'bg-orange-50 border-orange-200',
          icon: <AlertCircleIcon className="w-6 h-6 text-orange-600" />,
          label: 'En cours',
          textColor: 'text-orange-900',
        };
      case 'pending':
        return {
          color: 'bg-gray-50 border-gray-200',
          icon: <AlertCircleIcon className="w-6 h-6 text-gray-600" />,
          label: 'En attente',
          textColor: 'text-gray-900',
        };
      default:
        return {
          color: 'bg-gray-50 border-gray-200',
          icon: null,
          label: '',
          textColor: 'text-gray-900',
        };
    }
  };

  const config = getStatusConfig();

  return (
    <section
      className={`rounded-xl border-2 p-4 ${config.color}`}
      aria-label="État des paiements"
    >
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-4">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
          {config.icon}
          <div>
            <h2 className={`text-lg font-semibold ${config.textColor}`}>
              Paiement • {config.label}
            </h2>
            <p className="text-sm opacity-80">
              Total : {formatAmount(payment.total_amount_cents)}
            </p>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <EuroIcon className="w-8 h-8 opacity-50" />
      </div>

      {/* Progress Bar */}
      <div className="mb-4">
        <div className="flex justify-between text-sm mb-2">
          <span className="opacity-80">Payé</span>
          <span className="font-medium">
            {formatAmount(payment.paid_amount_cents)} / {formatAmount(payment.total_amount_cents)}
          </span>
        </div>
        
        <div className="w-full bg-gray-200 rounded-full h-3 overflow-hidden">
          <div
            className={`h-full rounded-full transition-all duration-500 ${
              payment.status === 'paid' ? 'bg-emerald-500' : 'bg-orange-500'
            }`}
            style={{ width: `${getProgressPercentage()}%` }}
            role="progressbar"
            aria-valuenow={getProgressPercentage()}
            aria-valuemin={0}
            aria-valuemax={100}
            aria-label="Progression du paiement"
          />
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Remaining Amount */}
      {payment.remaining_amount_cents > 0 && (
        <div className="bg-white/50 rounded-lg p-3">
          <p className="text-sm opacity-80 mb-1">Reste à payer</p>
          <p className="text-2xl font-bold">{formatAmount(payment.remaining_amount_cents)}</p>
        </div>
      )}
    </section>
  );
}
```

### 📁 `packages/web/app/dashboard/components/DocumentGrid.tsx`

```typescript
'use client';

import { DocumentSummary } from '@mon-omra/shared';
import { DocumentIcon, DownloadIcon, LockIcon } from '@/components/icons';
import { useDownloadDocument } from '@/hooks/useDocuments';
import { useState } from 'react';

interface DocumentGridProps {
  documents: DocumentSummary[];
}

export function DocumentGrid({ documents }: DocumentGridProps) {
  const { downloadDocument, isLoading, error } = useDownloadDocument();
  const [downloadingId, setDownloadingId] = useState<string | null>(null);

  const getDocumentIcon = (type: DocumentSummary['type']) => {
    switch (type) {
      case 'passport':
        return '🛂';
      case 'visa':
        return '📋';
      case 'ticket':
        return '✈️';
      case 'contract':
        return '📄';
      default:
        return '📁';
    }
  };

  const getDocumentLabel = (type: DocumentSummary['type']) => {
    const labels: Record<DocumentSummary['type'], string> = {
      passport: 'Passeport',
      visa: 'Visa',
      ticket: 'Billet d\'avion',
      contract: 'Contrat',
      other: 'Document',
    };
    return labels[type] || type;
  };

  const handleDownload = async (doc: DocumentSummary) => {
    setDownloadingId(doc.id);
    try {
      await downloadDocument(doc.id);
    } finally {
      setDownloadingId(null);
    }
  };

  const isExpired = (doc: DocumentSummary) => {
    if (!doc.expires_at) return false;
    return new Date(doc.expires_at) < new Date();
  };

  if (documents.length === 0) {
    return (
      <section className="bg-white rounded-xl border border-gray-200 p-6" aria-label="Documents">
        <div className="text-center">
          <DocumentIcon className="w-12 h-12 text-gray-300 mx-auto mb-3" />
          <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-1">
            Aucun document
          </h2>
          <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">
            Votre agence ajoutera les documents ici.
          </p>
        </div>
      </section>
    );
  }

  return (
    <section className="bg-white rounded-xl border border-gray-200 p-4" aria-label="Documents">
      <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-4">
        Mes documents ({documents.length})
      </h2>

      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 gap-3">
        {documents.map((doc) => {
          const expired = isExpired(doc);
          const isDownloading = downloadingId === doc.id;

          return (
            <div
              key={doc.id}
              className={`flex items-center gap-3 p-3 rounded-lg border transition-colors ${
                expired
                  ? 'bg-gray-50 border-gray-200 opacity-60'
                  : 'bg-gray-50 border-gray-200 hover:bg-gray-100'
              }`}
            >
              <span className="text-2xl flex-shrink-0" aria-hidden="true">
                {getDocumentIcon(doc.type)}
              </span>

              <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                <p className="font-medium text-gray-900 truncate">
                  {getDocumentLabel(doc.type)}
                </p>
                <p className="text-xs text-gray-500">
                  {new Date(doc.uploaded_at).toLocaleDateString('fr-FR')}
                </p>
                {expired && (
                  <p className="text-xs text-red-600 font-medium">
                    Expiré
                  </p>
                )}
              </div>

              <button
                onClick={() => handleDownload(doc)}
                disabled={expired || isLoading || isDownloading}
                className={`flex-shrink-0 p-2 rounded-lg transition-colors focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-500 focus:ring-offset-2 ${
                  expired
                    ? 'text-gray-400 cursor-not-allowed'
                    : isDownloading
                    ? 'text-gray-400'
                    : 'text-emerald-600 hover:bg-emerald-50'
                }`}
                aria-label={`Télécharger ${getDocumentLabel(doc.type)}`}
              >
                {isDownloading ? (
                  <div className="w-5 h-5 border-2 border-current border-t-transparent rounded-full animate-spin" />
                ) : expired ? (
                  <LockIcon className="w-5 h-5" />
                ) : (
                  <DownloadIcon className="w-5 h-5" />
                )}
              </button>
            </div>
          );
        })}
      </div>

      {error && (
        <div className="mt-4 p-3 bg-red-50 border border-red-200 rounded-lg text-sm text-red-900">
          Erreur lors du téléchargement. Veuillez réessayer.
        </div>
      )}
    </section>
  );
}
```

### 📁 `packages/web/hooks/usePilgrimDashboard.ts`

```typescript
import { useQuery } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { PilgrimDashboard } from '@mon-omra/shared';
import { apiClient } from '@/lib/api';

const QUERY_KEY = ['pilgrim-dashboard'];

async function fetchDashboard(): Promise<PilgrimDashboard> {
  const response = await apiClient.get('/api/v1/pilgrims/me/dashboard');
  
  if (!response.ok) {
    const error = await response.json();
    throw new Error(error.error?.message || 'Failed to fetch dashboard');
  }
  
  return response.json();
}

export function usePilgrimDashboard() {
  return useQuery<PilgrimDashboard, Error>({
    queryKey: QUERY_KEY,
    queryFn: fetchDashboard,
    staleTime: 5 * 60 * 1000, // 5 minutes
    retry: 3,
    retryDelay: (attemptIndex) => Math.min(1000 * 2 ** attemptIndex, 30000),
    refetchOnWindowFocus: true,
    refetchOnReconnect: true,
  });
}

export function invalidateDashboard() {
  // Called after mutations to refresh data
  return { type: 'INVALIDATE', queryKey: QUERY_KEY };
}
```

### 📁 `packages/web/hooks/useDocuments.ts`

```typescript
import { useMutation, useQueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { apiClient } from '@/lib/api';

interface DownloadUrlResponse {
  download_url: string;
  expires_in_sec: number;
  filename: string;
}

async function getDownloadUrl(documentId: string): Promise<DownloadUrlResponse> {
  const response = await apiClient.get(`/api/v1/documents/${documentId}/download-url`);
  
  if (!response.ok) {
    const error = await response.json();
    throw new Error(error.error?.message || 'Failed to get download URL');
  }
  
  return response.json();
}

export function useDownloadDocument() {
  const queryClient = useQueryClient();

  const mutation = useMutation({
    mutationFn: async (documentId: string) => {
      const { download_url, filename } = await getDownloadUrl(documentId);
      
      // Trigger download
      const link = document.createElement('a');
      link.href = download_url;
      link.download = filename;
      document.body.appendChild(link);
      link.click();
      document.body.removeChild(link);
      
      // Track download event
      import('@/lib/analytics').then(({ trackEvent }) => {
        trackEvent('document_downloaded', { document_id: documentId });
      });
    },
    onError: (error) => {
      console.error('Download failed:', error);
    },
  });

  return {
    downloadDocument: mutation.mutateAsync,
    isLoading: mutation.isPending,
    error: mutation.error,
  };
}
```

### 📁 `packages/web/components/ErrorBoundary.tsx`

```typescript
'use client';

import { Component, ErrorInfo, ReactNode } from 'react';
import { AlertCircleIcon } from './icons';

interface Props {
  children: ReactNode;
  error?: Error;
  onRetry?: () => void;
  title?: string;
  message?: string;
}

interface State {
  hasError: boolean;
  error: Error | null;
}

export class ErrorBoundary extends Component<Props, State> {
  public state: State = {
    hasError: false,
    error: null,
  };

  public static getDerivedStateFromError(error: Error): State {
    return { hasError: true, error };
  }

  public componentDidCatch(error: Error, errorInfo: ErrorInfo) {
    console.error('ErrorBoundary caught error:', error, errorInfo);
    
    // Log to error tracking service
    import('@/lib/analytics').then(({ trackEvent }) => {
      trackEvent('error_boundary_triggered', {
        error_name: error.name,
        error_message: error.message,
        component_stack: errorInfo.componentStack,
      });
    });
  }

  private handleRetry = () => {
    this.setState({ hasError: false, error: null });
    this.props.onRetry?.();
  };

  public render() {
    if (this.state.hasError || this.props.error) {
      const error = this.state.error || this.props.error;
      const title = this.props.title || 'Une erreur est survenue';
      const message = this.props.message || error?.message || 'Veuillez réessayer.';

      return (
        <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center p-4 bg-gray-50">
          <div className="max-w-md w-full bg-white rounded-xl border border-gray-200 p-6 text-center">
            <AlertCircleIcon className="w-12 h-12 text-red-500 mx-auto mb-4" />
            
            <h1 className="text-xl font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-2">
              {title}
            </h1>
            
            <p className="text-gray-600 mb-6">
              {message}
            </p>
            
            {this.props.onRetry && (
              <button
                onClick={this.handleRetry}
                className="inline-flex items-center justify-center px-6 py-3 bg-emerald-600 text-white font-medium rounded-lg hover:bg-emerald-700 transition-colors focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-500 focus:ring-offset-2"
              >
                Réessayer
              </button>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
      );
    }

    return this.props.children;
  }
}
```
