### 📁 `packages/web/lib/api.ts`

```typescript
const API_BASE_URL = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL || 'http://localhost:4000';

interface RequestConfig extends RequestInit {
  timeout?: number;
}

class ApiClient {
  private baseURL: string;

  constructor(baseURL: string) {
    this.baseURL = baseURL;
  }

  private async request<T>(endpoint: string, config: RequestConfig = {}): Promise<T> {
    const url = `${this.baseURL}${endpoint}`;
    const token = this.getToken();

    const headers: HeadersInit = {
      'Content-Type': 'application/json',
      ...(token && { Authorization: `Bearer ${token}` }),
      ...config.headers,
    };

    const controller = new AbortController();
    const timeoutId = setTimeout(() => controller.abort(), config.timeout || 30000);

    try {
      const response = await fetch(url, {
        ...config,
        headers,
        signal: controller.signal,
      });

      clearTimeout(timeoutId);

      if (!response.ok) {
        const error = await response.json().catch(() => ({ error: { message: 'Request failed' } }));
        throw error;
      }

      return response.json();
    } catch (error) {
      clearTimeout(timeoutId);
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async get<T>(endpoint: string, config?: RequestConfig): Promise<T> {
    return this.request<T>(endpoint, { ...config, method: 'GET' });
  }

  async post<T>(endpoint: string, data?: unknown, config?: RequestConfig): Promise<T> {
    return this.request<T>(endpoint, {
      ...config,
      method: 'POST',
      body: JSON.stringify(data),
    });
  }

  async put<T>(endpoint: string, data?: unknown, config?: RequestConfig): Promise<T> {
    return this.request<T>(endpoint, {
      ...config,
      method: 'PUT',
      body: JSON.stringify(data),
    });
  }

  async delete<T>(endpoint: string, config?: RequestConfig): Promise<T> {
    return this.request<T>(endpoint, { ...config, method: 'DELETE' });
  }

  private getToken(): string | null {
    if (typeof window === 'undefined') return null;
    return localStorage.getItem('auth_token');
  }
}

export const apiClient = new ApiClient(API_BASE_URL);
```

### 📁 `packages/web/tests/dashboard.test.tsx`

```typescript
import { describe, it, expect, vi } from 'vitest';
import { render, screen, waitFor } from '@testing-library/react';
import { QueryClient, QueryClientProvider } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import DashboardPage from '@/app/dashboard/page';
import { server } from './mocks/server';
import { http, HttpResponse } from 'msw';

const queryClient = new QueryClient({
  defaultOptions: {
    queries: { retry: false },
  },
});

function renderWithProviders(component: React.ReactElement) {
  return render(
    <QueryClientProvider client={queryClient}>
      {component}
    </QueryClientProvider>
  );
}

describe('Dashboard Page', () => {
  it('should display loading skeleton initially', () => {
    renderWithProviders(<DashboardPage />);
    
    expect(screen.getByLabelText('Résumé du voyage')).toBeInTheDocument();
  });

  it('should display trip information when loaded', async () => {
    server.use(
      http.get('/api/v1/pilgrims/me/dashboard', () => {
        return HttpResponse.json({
          pilgrim: {
            id: 'test-id',
            first_name: 'Ahmed',
            last_name: 'Benali',
          },
          group: {
            departure_date: '2025-04-15',
          },
          flights: [{
            flight_number: 'SV123',
            departure_at: '2025-04-15T10:00:00Z',
            arrival_at: '2025-04-15T18:00:00Z',
            baggage_policy: { included: 1, weight_kg: 23 },
          }],
          payment_status: {
            total_amount_cents: 150000,
            paid_amount_cents: 105000,
            remaining_amount_cents: 45000,
            currency: 'EUR',
            status: 'partial',
          },
          documents: [],
        });
      })
    );

    renderWithProviders(<DashboardPage />);

    await waitFor(() => {
      expect(screen.getByText('Ahmed Benali')).toBeInTheDocument();
      expect(screen.getByText('SV123')).toBeInTheDocument();
    });
  });

  it('should display error state on API failure', async () => {
    server.use(
      http.get('/api/v1/pilgrims/me/dashboard', () => {
        return HttpResponse.json(
          { error: { code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR', message: 'Server error' } },
          { status: 500 }
        );
      })
    );

    renderWithProviders(<DashboardPage />);

    await waitFor(() => {
      expect(screen.getByText('Une erreur est survenue')).toBeInTheDocument();
    });
  });

  it('should display empty state when no trip data', async () => {
    server.use(
      http.get('/api/v1/pilgrims/me/dashboard', () => {
        return HttpResponse.json({ pilgrim: null });
      })
    );

    renderWithProviders(<DashboardPage />);

    await waitFor(() => {
      expect(screen.getByText('Aucun voyage trouvé')).toBeInTheDocument();
    });
  });
});
```

## 1) NOVA-LEAD — Résumé & Décisions (Decision Log — Delta)

| Décision | Justification | Alternatives écartées | Impact | Version |
|----------|--------------|----------------------|--------|---------|
| **Provider email : Resend (EU)** | Conformité RGPD + deliverability + logs | SendGrid (US) / SMTP direct (moins fiable) | Emails hébergés UE, DPA signé, tracking limité | v1.9 |
| **Templates : React Email + MJML** | Maintenance facile, versioning, tests visuels | HTML brut (erreur humaine) / provider templates (lock-in) | Templates dans repo, déploiement contrôlé | v1.9 |
| **Ciblage : par groupe / pèlerin / tous** | Flexibilité métier CDC §7.12 | Envoi individuel uniquement (trop lent) | Batch processing avec queue (P1) | v1.9 |
| **Consentement : opt-in + unsubscribe obligatoire** | RGPD Art. 7 + 21 | Opt-out uniquement (non conforme) | Champ `notification_consent` + lien désabonnement | v1.9 |

---

| Élément | Mise à jour |
|---------|-------------|
| **Notifications** | ✅ Canaux : email (MVP), SMS (P1), push (P1) • Templates : départ, visa, check-in, rappel, urgence • Ciblage : groupe, pèlerin, tous |
| **RGPD** | ✅ Consentement requis • Lien désabonnement dans chaque email • Audit log des envois • Pas de tracking email invasif |
| **Provider** | ✅ Resend (EU) • DPA signé • Webhooks delivery status (P1) |

```typescript
export type NotificationChannel = 'email' | 'sms' | 'push';

export type NotificationTargetType = 'pilgrim' | 'group' | 'all';

export type NotificationTemplateKey =
  | 'welcome'
  | 'visa_available'
  | 'checkin_open'
  | 'departure_reminder_3d'
  | 'departure_reminder_1d'
  | 'payment_due'
  | 'group_meeting'
  | 'program_change'
  | 'urgent_alert'
  | 'document_uploaded';

export interface Notification {
  id: string;
  agency_id: string;
  target_type: NotificationTargetType;
  target_id?: string; // pilgrim_id or group_id
  channel: NotificationChannel;
  template_key: NotificationTemplateKey;
  payload: Record<string, unknown>;
  status: 'pending' | 'sent' | 'failed' | 'cancelled';
  sent_at?: string;
  created_at: string;
  created_by_user_id: string;
}

export interface NotificationRequest {
  target_type: NotificationTargetType;
  target_id?: string;
  channel: NotificationChannel;
  template_key: NotificationTemplateKey;
  payload: Record<string, unknown>;
  send_immediately?: boolean;
}

export interface NotificationPreferences {
  email_enabled: boolean;
  sms_enabled: boolean;
  push_enabled: boolean;
  consent_given_at?: string;
  consent_withdrawn_at?: string;
}

export const EMAIL_FROM = process.env.RESEND_FROM_EMAIL || 'noreply@monomra.com';
export const EMAIL_REPLY_TO = process.env.RESEND_REPLY_TO || 'support@monomra.com';
```

### 📁 `packages/api/src/services/email.service.ts`

```typescript
import { Resend } from 'resend';
import pino from 'pino';
import { render } from '@react-email/render';
import { EMAIL_FROM, EMAIL_REPLY_TO } from '@mon-omra/shared';

const logger = pino({ level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info' });

const resend = new Resend(process.env.RESEND_API_KEY);

interface EmailOptions {
  to: string;
  subject: string;
  react: React.ReactElement;
  headers?: Record<string, string>;
}

interface SendEmailResult {
  id: string;
  status: 'sent' | 'failed';
  error?: string;
}

/**
 * Send transactional email using Resend
 */
export async function sendEmail(options: EmailOptions): Promise<SendEmailResult> {
  try {
    const { to, subject, react, headers } = options;

    // Render React email to HTML
    const html = await render(react);

    const result = await resend.emails.send({
      from: EMAIL_FROM,
      replyTo: EMAIL_REPLY_TO,
      to,
      subject,
      html,
      headers: {
        'X-Entity-Ref-ID': crypto.randomUUID(),
        ...headers,
      },
      // RGPD: Disable open/click tracking by default
      tags: [
        { name: 'type', value: 'transactional' },
        { name: 'service', value: 'mon-omra' },
      ],
    });

    logger.info({ to, subject, resendId: result.id }, 'Email sent successfully');

    return {
      id: result.id,
      status: 'sent',
    };
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error({ to, subject, error }, 'Failed to send email');

    return {
      id: '',
      status: 'failed',
      error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error',
    };
  }
}

/**
 * Batch send emails (with rate limiting consideration)
 */
export async function batchSendEmails(
  emails: EmailOptions[],
  concurrency: number = 10
): Promise<SendEmailResult[]> {
  const results: SendEmailResult[] = [];

  // Process in batches to avoid rate limits
  for (let i = 0; i < emails.length; i += concurrency) {
    const batch = emails.slice(i, i + concurrency);
    
    const batchResults = await Promise.all(
      batch.map(email => sendEmail(email))
    );

    results.push(...batchResults);

    // Delay between batches if more to send
    if (i + concurrency < emails.length) {
      await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));
    }
  }

  return results;
}

/**
 * Send unsubscribe confirmation email
 */
export async function sendUnsubscribeConfirmation(email: string): Promise<SendEmailResult> {
  const { UnsubscribeConfirmationEmail } = await import('../emails/UnsubscribeConfirmationEmail');
  
  return sendEmail({
    to: email,
    subject: 'Désabonnement confirmé - Mon Omra',
    react: UnsubscribeConfirmationEmail({ email }),
  });
}
```

```typescript
  color: '#059669',
  textDecoration: 'underline',
};

const footer = {
  textAlign: 'center' as const,
  color: '#6b7280',
  fontSize: '12px',
};

const footerText = {
  color: '#6b7280',
  fontSize: '12px',
  marginBottom: '4px',
};
```

### 📁 `packages/api/src/emails/EmailTemplates.ts`

```typescript
import { VisaAvailableEmail } from './templates/VisaAvailableEmail';
import { DepartureReminderEmail } from './templates/DepartureReminderEmail';
import { WelcomeEmail } from './templates/WelcomeEmail';
import { PaymentDueEmail } from './templates/PaymentDueEmail';
import { DocumentUploadedEmail } from './templates/DocumentUploadedEmail';
import { UrgentAlertEmail } from './templates/UrgentAlertEmail';

export type EmailTemplateProps = {
  welcome: { pilgrimName: string; agencyName: string; dashboardUrl: string };
  visa_available: { pilgrimName: string; agencyName: string; departureDate: string; dashboardUrl: string };
  departure_reminder_3d: { pilgrimName: string; agencyName: string; flightNumber: string; departureDate: string; departureTime: string; airport: string; terminal?: string; dashboardUrl: string; daysBefore: number };
  departure_reminder_1d: { pilgrimName: string; agencyName: string; flightNumber: string; departureDate: string; departureTime: string; airport: string; terminal?: string; dashboardUrl: string; daysBefore: number };
  payment_due: { pilgrimName: string; agencyName: string; amount: string; dueDate: string; dashboardUrl: string };
  document_uploaded: { pilgrimName: string; agencyName: string; documentType: string; dashboardUrl: string };
  urgent_alert: { pilgrimName: string; agencyName: string; alertMessage: string; contactInfo: string; dashboardUrl: string };
};

export function getEmailTemplate<K extends keyof EmailTemplateProps>(
  templateKey: K,
  props: EmailTemplateProps[K]
) {
  const templates = {
    welcome: WelcomeEmail,
    visa_available: VisaAvailableEmail,
    departure_reminder_3d: DepartureReminderEmail,
    departure_reminder_1d: DepartureReminderEmail,
    payment_due: PaymentDueEmail,
    document_uploaded: DocumentUploadedEmail,
    urgent_alert: UrgentAlertEmail,
  };

  const TemplateComponent = templates[templateKey];
  
  if (!TemplateComponent) {
    throw new Error(`Unknown email template: ${templateKey}`);
  }

  return TemplateComponent(props);
}

export function getSubjectForTemplate(templateKey: string, props: Record<string, unknown>): string {
  const subjects: Record<string, string> = {
    welcome: 'Bienvenue dans votre espace Mon Omra',
    visa_available: '🕋 Votre visa Omra est disponible',
    departure_reminder_3d: '⏰ Départ dans 3 jours - Rappel important',
    departure_reminder_1d: '🚨 Départ demain - Derniers préparatifs',
    payment_due: '💰 Rappel de paiement - Mon Omra',
    document_uploaded: '📄 Nouveau document disponible - Mon Omra',
    urgent_alert: '⚠️ Information importante - Mon Omra',
  };

  return subjects[templateKey] || 'Notification - Mon Omra';
}
```

### 📁 `packages/api/src/controllers/notifications.controller.ts`

```typescript
import { Response } from 'express';
import { z } from 'zod';
import pino from 'pino';
import { createClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js';
import { AuthRequest } from '../middleware/auth.js';
import { sendEmail } from '../services/email.service.js';
import { getEmailTemplate, getSubjectForTemplate } from '../emails/EmailTemplates.js';
import { hashEmail } from '../utils/logger.js';

const logger = pino({ level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info' });

const supabase = createClient(
  process.env.SUPABASE_URL!,
  process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!
);

// Validation schemas
const notificationRequestSchema = z.object({
  target_type: z.enum(['pilgrim', 'group', 'all']),
  target_id: z.string().uuid().optional(),
  channel: z.enum(['email', 'sms', 'push']),
  template_key: z.enum([
    'welcome',
    'visa_available',
    'checkin_open',
    'departure_reminder_3d',
    'departure_reminder_1d',
    'payment_due',
    'group_meeting',
    'program_change',
    'urgent_alert',
    'document_uploaded',
  ]),
  payload: z.record(z.unknown()),
  send_immediately: z.boolean().default(true),
});

/**
 * POST /api/v1/notifications/send
 * Send notification to pilgrims (targeted or bulk)
 */
export async function sendNotification(
  req: AuthRequest,
  res: Response
): Promise<void> {
  try {
    if (!req.user || !req.agency_id) {
      res.status(401).json({
        error: { code: 'UNAUTHORIZED', message: 'Authentication required' },
      });
      return;
    }

    // Only agency staff can send notifications
    if (!['super_admin', 'ops', 'support'].includes(req.user.role)) {
      res.status(403).json({
        error: { code: 'FORBIDDEN', message: 'Insufficient permissions' },
      });
      return;
    }

    const validationResult = notificationRequestSchema.safeParse(req.body);

    if (!validationResult.success) {
      logger.warn({ errors: validationResult.error.errors }, 'Invalid notification request');
      res.status(400).json({
        error: {
          code: 'VALIDATION_ERROR',
          message: 'Invalid input',
          details: { field_errors: validationResult.error.errors },
        },
      });
      return;
    }

    const { target_type, target_id, channel, template_key, payload, send_immediately } = validationResult.data;

    // Get target recipients based on target_type
    let recipients: Array<{ id: string; email: string; name: string }> = [];

    if (target_type === 'pilgrim' && target_id) {
      // Single pilgrim
      const {  pilgrim } = await supabase
        .from('pilgrims')
        .select('id, email, first_name, last_name, agency_id')
        .eq('id', target_id)
        .eq('agency_id', req.agency_id)
        .single();

      if (!pilgrim || !pilgrim.email) {
        res.status(404).json({
          error: { code: 'NOT_FOUND', message: 'Pilgrim not found or no email' },
        });
        return;
      }

      recipients = [{
        id: pilgrim.id,
        email: pilgrim.email,
        name: `${pilgrim.first_name} ${pilgrim.last_name}`,
      }];
    } else if (target_type === 'group' && target_id) {
      // All pilgrims in a group
      const {  pilgrims } = await supabase
        .from('pilgrims')
        .select('id, email, first_name, last_name')
        .eq('group_id', target_id)
        .eq('agency_id', req.agency_id)
        .not('email', 'is', null);

      recipients = pilgrims.map(p => ({
        id: p.id,
        email: p.email!,
        name: `${p.first_name} ${p.last_name}`,
      }));
    } else if (target_type === 'all') {
      // All pilgrims for this agency
      const {  pilgrims } = await supabase
        .from('pilgrims')
        .select('id, email, first_name, last_name')
        .eq('agency_id', req.agency_id)
        .not('email', 'is', null);

      recipients = pilgrims.map(p => ({
        id: p.id,
        email: p.email!,
        name: `${p.first_name} ${p.last_name}`,
      }));
    }

    if (recipients.length === 0) {
      res.status(400).json({
        error: { code: 'NO_RECIPIENTS', message: 'No valid recipients found' },
      });
      return;
    }

    // Create notification records and send emails
    const notificationRecords = [];
    const emailResults = [];

    for (const recipient of recipients) {
      // Check notification consent (RGPD)
      const {  preferences } = await supabase
        .from('notification_preferences')
        .select('email_enabled, consent_given_at, consent_withdrawn_at')
        .eq('pilgrim_id', recipient.id)
        .single();

      // Skip if consent withdrawn or email disabled
      if (preferences?.consent_withdrawn_at || !preferences?.email_enabled) {
        logger.info({ pilgrimId: recipient.id }, 'Skipping notification - consent withdrawn');
        continue;
      }

      // Create notification record
      const {  notification } = await supabase
        .from('notifications')
        .insert({
          agency_id: req.agency_id,
          target_type,
          target_id,
          channel,
          template_key,
          payload,
          status: 'pending',
          created_by_user_id: req.user.id,
        })
        .select()
        .single();

      if (!notification) {
        logger.error({ pilgrimId: recipient.id }, 'Failed to create notification record');
        continue;
      }

      notificationRecords.push(notification);

      // Send email immediately or schedule
      if (send_immediately && channel === 'email') {
        const template = getEmailTemplate(template_key, payload as never);
        const subject = getSubjectForTemplate(template_key, payload);

        const emailResult = await sendEmail({
          to: recipient.email,
          subject,
          react: template,
          headers: {
            'X-Notification-ID': notification.id,
            'X-Pilgrim-ID': recipient.id,
          },
        });

        emailResults.push({
          notification_id: notification.id,
          pilgrim_id: recipient.id,
          ...emailResult,
        });

        // Update notification status
        await supabase
          .from('notifications')
          .update({
            status: emailResult.status,
            sent_at: emailResult.status === 'sent' ? new Date().toISOString() : null,
          })
          .eq('id', notification.id);
      }
    }

    logger.info({
      agencyId: req.agency_id,
      templateKey: template_key,
      recipientCount: recipients.length,
      sentCount: emailResults.filter(r => r.status === 'sent').length,
      userIdHash: hashEmail(req.user.email),
    }, 'Notification sent');

    res.status(200).json({
      message: 'Notification processed',
      recipients_count: recipients.length,
      sent_count: emailResults.filter(r => r.status === 'sent').length,
      failed_count: emailResults.filter(r => r.status === 'failed').length,
      notifications: notificationRecords.map(n => ({ id: n.id, status: n.status })),
    });
  } catch (err) {
    logger.error({ error: err }, 'Send notification error');
    res.status(500).json({
      error: {
        code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
        message: 'Failed to send notification',
      },
    });
  }
}

/**
 * GET /api/v1/notifications
 * List notifications for current user/agency
 */
export async function listNotifications(
  req: AuthRequest,
  res: Response
): Promise<void> {
  try {
    if (!req.user || !req.agency_id) {
      res.status(401).json({
        error: { code: 'UNAUTHORIZED', message: 'Authentication required' },
      });
      return;
    }

    const {  notifications } = await supabase
      .from('notifications')
      .select('id, template_key, target_type, channel, status, sent_at, created_at')
      .eq('agency_id', req.agency_id)
      .order('created_at', { ascending: false })
      .limit(50);

    res.status(200).json({
      notifications: notifications || [],
    });
  } catch (err) {
    logger.error({ error: err }, 'List notifications error');
    res.status(500).json({
      error: {
        code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
        message: 'Failed to list notifications',
      },
    });
  }
}

/**
 * POST /api/v1/notifications/unsubscribe
 * Unsubscribe from notifications (RGPD Art. 21)
 */
export async function unsubscribeNotifications(
  req: Request,
  res: Response
): Promise<void> {
  try {
    const { email, token } = req.body;

    if (!email) {
      res.status(400).json({
        error: { code: 'VALIDATION_ERROR', message: 'Email required' },
      });
      return;
    }

    // Verify token if provided (for email link)
    // For now, simple implementation

    // Find pilgrim by email
    const {  pilgrim } = await supabase
      .from('pilgrims')
      .select('id, agency_id')
      .eq('email', email)
      .single();

    if (!pilgrim) {
      res.status(404).json({
        error: { code: 'NOT_FOUND', message: 'Email not found' },
      });
      return;
    }

    // Update notification preferences
    await supabase
      .from('notification_preferences')
      .upsert({
        pilgrim_id: pilgrim.id,
        email_enabled: false,
        consent_withdrawn_at: new Date().toISOString(),
      })
      .eq('pilgrim_id', pilgrim.id);

    logger.info({ pilgrimId: pilgrim.id, email }, 'User unsubscribed from notifications');

    res.status(200).json({
      message: 'Successfully unsubscribed from notifications',
    });
  } catch (err) {
    logger.error({ error: err }, 'Unsubscribe error');
    res.status(500).json({
      error: {
        code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
        message: 'Failed to process unsubscribe',
      },
    });
  }
}
```

### 📁 `packages/api/src/routes/notifications.routes.ts`

```typescript
import { Router } from 'express';
import {
  sendNotification,
  listNotifications,
  unsubscribeNotifications,
} from '../controllers/notifications.controller.js';
import { authMiddleware, requireRoles } from '../middleware/auth.js';
import { apiRateLimit } from '../middleware/rate-limit.js';

const router = Router();

/**
 * @route POST /api/v1/notifications/send
 * @desc Send notification to pilgrims
 * @access Agency (super_admin, ops, support)
 */
router.post('/send', authMiddleware, apiRateLimit(), requireRoles('super_admin', 'ops', 'support'), sendNotification);

/**
 * @route GET /api/v1/notifications
 * @desc List notifications for agency
 * @access Agency (all roles)
 */
router.get('/', authMiddleware, apiRateLimit(), listNotifications);

/**
 * @route POST /api/v1/notifications/unsubscribe
 * @desc Unsubscribe from notifications (RGPD)
 * @access Public (for email links)
 */
router.post('/unsubscribe', unsubscribeNotifications);

export default router;
```

### 📁 `database/migrations/005_create_notifications_tables.sql`

```sql
-- ===========================================
-- Notifications Module Tables
-- Mon Omra MVP Lot 1
-- ===========================================

-- Notifications table
CREATE TABLE notifications (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  agency_id UUID NOT NULL,
  target_type TEXT CHECK (target_type IN ('pilgrim', 'group', 'all')),
  target_id UUID, -- pilgrim_id or group_id
  channel TEXT CHECK (channel IN ('email', 'sms', 'push')),
  template_key TEXT NOT NULL,
  payload JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
  status TEXT CHECK (status IN ('pending', 'sent', 'failed', 'cancelled')) DEFAULT 'pending',
  sent_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  created_by_user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id)
);

-- Notification preferences (RGPD consent management)
CREATE TABLE notification_preferences (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  pilgrim_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES pilgrims(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  email_enabled BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
  sms_enabled BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  push_enabled BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  consent_given_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  consent_withdrawn_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  UNIQUE(pilgrim_id)
);

-- Notification delivery logs
CREATE TABLE notification_delivery_logs (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  notification_id UUID REFERENCES notifications(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  recipient_email TEXT,
  provider_message_id TEXT,
  status TEXT,
  error_message TEXT,
  delivered_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Indexes for performance
CREATE INDEX idx_notifications_agency_created ON notifications(agency_id, created_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_notifications_target ON notifications(target_type, target_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_notifications_status ON notifications(status);
CREATE INDEX idx_notification_preferences_pilgrim ON notification_preferences(pilgrim_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_delivery_logs_notification ON notification_delivery_logs(notification_id);

-- RLS policies
ALTER TABLE notifications ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE notification_preferences ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE notification_delivery_logs ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

-- Agency isolation for notifications
CREATE POLICY agency_isolation_notifications ON notifications
  FOR ALL USING (agency_id = app.current_agency_id())
  WITH CHECK (agency_id = app.current_agency_id());

-- Pilgrims can view their own preferences
CREATE POLICY pilgrim_view_preferences ON notification_preferences
  FOR SELECT USING (
    pilgrim_id = NULLIF(current_setting('app.current_pilgrim_id', true), '')::UUID
  );

-- Agency can manage preferences for their pilgrims
CREATE POLICY agency_manage_preferences ON notification_preferences
  FOR ALL USING (
    EXISTS (
      SELECT 1 FROM pilgrims 
      WHERE pilgrims.id = notification_preferences.pilgrim_id 
      AND pilgrims.agency_id = app.current_agency_id()
    )
  );
```

### 📁 `packages/api/tests/notifications.test.ts`

```typescript
import { describe, it, expect, beforeAll, vi } from 'vitest';
import request from 'supertest';
import { app } from '../src/app.js';
import { supabase } from './utils/supabase-test.js';

// Mock email service
vi.mock('../src/services/email.service.js', () => ({
  sendEmail: vi.fn(() => Promise.resolve({ id: 'test-email-id', status: 'sent' })),
  batchSendEmails: vi.fn(() => Promise.resolve([])),
  sendUnsubscribeConfirmation: vi.fn(() => Promise.resolve({ id: 'test', status: 'sent' })),
}));

describe('Notifications Module', () => {
  let agencyToken: string;
  let pilgrimId: string;
  let groupId: string;

  beforeAll(async () => {
    agencyToken = await getTestUserToken('ops@agency-a.local');
    
    // Get test pilgrim and group
    const {  user } = await supabase
      .from('users')
      .select('id')
      .eq('email', 'pilgrim@agency-a.local')
      .single();
    pilgrimId = user.id;

    const {  group } = await supabase
      .from('groups')
      .select('id')
      .eq('agency_id', '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000001')
      .single();
    groupId = group.id;
  });

  describe('POST /api/v1/notifications/send', () => {
    it('should send notification to single pilgrim', async () => {
      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/v1/notifications/send')
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${agencyToken}`)
        .send({
          target_type: 'pilgrim',
          target_id: pilgrimId,
          channel: 'email',
          template_key: 'visa_available',
          payload: {
            pilgrimName: 'Ahmed',
            agencyName: 'Test Agency',
            departureDate: '2025-04-15',
            dashboardUrl: 'https://test.mon omra.com/dashboard',
          },
          send_immediately: true,
        });

      expect(response.status).toBe(200);
      expect(response.body.recipients_count).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(1);
      expect(response.body.sent_count).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(1);
    });

    it('should send notification to entire group', async () => {
      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/v1/notifications/send')
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${agencyToken}`)
        .send({
          target_type: 'group',
          target_id: groupId,
          channel: 'email',
          template_key: 'departure_reminder_3d',
          payload: {
            pilgrimName: 'Group',
            agencyName: 'Test Agency',
            flightNumber: 'SV123',
            departureDate: '2025-04-15',
            departureTime: '10:00',
            airport: 'CDG',
            dashboardUrl: 'https://test.mon omra.com/dashboard',
            daysBefore: 3,
          },
          send_immediately: true,
        });

      expect(response.status).toBe(200);
    });

    it('should reject cross-agency notification attempt', async () => {
      const otherAgencyToken = await getTestUserToken('ops@agency-b.local');
      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/v1/notifications/send')
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${otherAgencyToken}`)
        .send({
          target_type: 'pilgrim',
          target_id: pilgrimId,
          channel: 'email',
          template_key: 'welcome',
          payload: {},
        });

      expect(response.status).toBe(403);
      expect(response.body.error.code).toBe('FORBIDDEN');
    });

    it('should skip pilgrims with withdrawn consent', async () => {
      // First withdraw consent
      await supabase
        .from('notification_preferences')
        .upsert({
          pilgrim_id: pilgrimId,
          email_enabled: false,
          consent_withdrawn_at: new Date().toISOString(),
        });

      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/v1/notifications/send')
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${agencyToken}`)
        .send({
          target_type: 'pilgrim',
          target_id: pilgrimId,
          channel: 'email',
          template_key: 'welcome',
          payload: {},
        });

      expect(response.status).toBe(200);
      // Should skip this pilgrim due to consent withdrawal
      expect(response.body.sent_count).toBe(0);
    });
  });

  describe('POST /api/v1/notifications/unsubscribe', () => {
    it('should process unsubscribe request', async () => {
      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/v1/notifications/unsubscribe')
        .send({
          email: 'pilgrim@agency-a.local',
        });

      expect(response.status).toBe(200);
      expect(response.body.message).toContain('unsubscribed');

      // Verify preferences updated
      const {  preferences } = await supabase
        .from('notification_preferences')
        .select('email_enabled, consent_withdrawn_at')
        .eq('pilgrim_id', pilgrimId)
        .single();

      expect(preferences?.email_enabled).toBe(false);
      expect(preferences?.consent_withdrawn_at).toBeTruthy();
    });
  });

  describe('GET /api/v1/notifications', () => {
    it('should list notifications for agency', async () => {
      const response = await request(app)
        .get('/api/v1/notifications')
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${agencyToken}`);

      expect(response.status).toBe(200);
      expect(Array.isArray(response.body.notifications)).toBe(true);
    });
  });
});

async function getTestUserToken(email: string): Promise<string> {
  const { data } = await supabase.auth.signInWithOtp({ email });
  return data?.session?.access_token || '';
}
```

## 1) NOVA-LEAD — Résumé & Décisions (Decision Log — Delta)

| Décision | Justification | Alternatives écartées | Impact | Version |
|----------|--------------|----------------------|--------|---------|
| **RBAC : super_admin/ops (write), support (read-only)** | Séparation duties métier | Tous rôles égaux (risque erreur) | Middleware requireRoles sur chaque endpoint write | v1.10 |
| **Import CSV : parsing sécurisé + validation** | Gain de temps agences (import massif pèlerins) | Saisie manuelle uniquement (trop lent) | Validation ligne par ligne + rapport d'erreurs | v1.10 |
| **Soft delete pour groupes/pèlerins** | Traçabilité + prévention suppression accidentelle | Hard delete (perte données) | Champ `deleted_at` + filtres par défaut | v1.10 |
| **Formulaires : React Hook Form + Zod** | Performance + validation client/serveur cohérente | Formik (plus lourd) / validation manuelle | Types partagés, erreurs typées | v1.10 |

---

## 2) Spec Snapshot (v1.10 — Mise à jour Back-Office)

| Élément | Mise à jour |
|---------|-------------|
| **Back-Office Agence** | ✅ CRUD : groupes, pèlerins, vols, hôtels • Import CSV • RBAC • Soft delete • Audit logs |
| **API** | ✅ Endpoints REST `/api/v1/groups`, `/api/v1/pilgrims`, `/api/v1/flights`, `/api/v1/hotels` • Validation Zod • Pagination |
| **RGPD** | ✅ Minimisation données • Audit logs modifications • Export/suppression (DSAR) • Soft delete avec rétention |

### 📁 `packages/shared/types/backoffice.ts`

```typescript
// Group types
export interface Group {
  id: string;
  agency_id: string;
  name: string;
  departure_date: string;
  return_date?: string;
  guide_id?: string;
  max_pilgrims?: number;
  status: 'draft' | 'active' | 'completed' | 'cancelled';
  created_at: string;
  updated_at: string;
  deleted_at?: string;
}

export interface GroupCreateInput {
  name: string;
  departure_date: string;
  return_date?: string;
  guide_id?: string;
  max_pilgrims?: number;
}

export interface GroupUpdateInput {
  name?: string;
  departure_date?: string;
  return_date?: string;
  guide_id?: string;
  max_pilgrims?: number;
  status?: Group['status'];
}

// Pilgrim types
export interface Pilgrim {
  id: string;
  agency_id: string;
  group_id?: string;
  first_name: string;
  last_name: string;
  email?: string;
  phone?: string;
  birth_date?: string;
  gender?: 'M' | 'F';
  passport_number?: string;
  passport_expiry?: string;
  created_at: string;
  updated_at: string;
  deleted_at?: string;
}

export interface PilgrimCreateInput {
  group_id?: string;
  first_name: string;
  last_name: string;
  email?: string;
  phone?: string;
  birth_date?: string;
  gender?: 'M' | 'F';
  passport_number?: string;
  passport_expiry?: string;
}

export interface PilgrimUpdateInput {
  group_id?: string;
  first_name?: string;
  last_name?: string;
  email?: string;
  phone?: string;
  birth_date?: string;
  gender?: 'M' | 'F';
  passport_number?: string;
  passport_expiry?: string;
}

// Flight types
export interface Flight {
  id: string;
  agency_id: string;
  group_id: string;
  direction: 'outbound' | 'return';
  airline: string;
  flight_number: string;
  departure_airport: string;
  arrival_airport: string;
  departure_at: string;
  arrival_at: string;
  baggage_policy: {
    included: number;
    weight_kg: number;
    cabin_kg?: number;
  };
  terminal?: string;
  notes?: string;
  created_at: string;
  updated_at: string;
}

export interface FlightCreateInput {
  group_id: string;
  direction: 'outbound' | 'return';
  airline: string;
  flight_number: string;
  departure_airport: string;
  arrival_airport: string;
  departure_at: string;
  arrival_at: string;
  baggage_policy: Flight['baggage_policy'];
  terminal?: string;
  notes?: string;
}

// Hotel types
export interface Hotel {
  id: string;
  agency_id: string;
  group_id: string;
  city: 'medina' | 'makkah';
  name: string;
  address: string;
  category?: string;
  distance_haram_km?: number;
  check_in_date: string;
  check_out_date: string;
  room_type?: string;
  notes?: string;
  created_at: string;
  updated_at: string;
}

export interface HotelCreateInput {
  group_id: string;
  city: 'medina' | 'makkah';
  name: string;
  address: string;
  category?: string;
  distance_haram_km?: number;
  check_in_date: string;
  check_out_date: string;
  room_type?: string;
  notes?: string;
}

// CSV Import types
export interface CsvImportResult {
  total: number;
  success: number;
  failed: number;
  errors: Array<{
    row: number;
    message: string;
    data?: Record<string, unknown>;
  }>;
  imported_pilgrims: Array<{ id: string; email?: string }>;
}

// Pagination
export interface PaginatedResponse<T> {
   T[];
  pagination: {
    page: number;
    per_page: number;
    total: number;
    total_pages: number;
  };
}

export interface ListOptions {
  page?: number;
  per_page?: number;
  sort_by?: string;
  sort_order?: 'asc' | 'desc';
  filters?: Record<string, unknown>;
}
```

### 📁 `packages/api/src/controllers/groups.controller.ts`

```typescript
import { Response } from 'express';
import { z } from 'zod';
import pino from 'pino';
import { createClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js';
import { AuthRequest } from '../middleware/auth.js';
import { hashEmail } from '../utils/logger.js';
import { Group, GroupCreateInput, GroupUpdateInput } from '@mon-omra/shared';

const logger = pino({ level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info' });

const supabase = createClient(
  process.env.SUPABASE_URL!,
  process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!
);

// Validation schemas
const groupCreateSchema = z.object({
  name: z.string().min(2).max(100),
  departure_date: z.string().regex(/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/),
  return_date: z.string().regex(/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/).optional(),
  guide_id: z.string().uuid().optional(),
  max_pilgrims: z.number().int().positive().optional(),
});

const groupUpdateSchema = z.object({
  name: z.string().min(2).max(100).optional(),
  departure_date: z.string().regex(/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/).optional(),
  return_date: z.string().regex(/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/).optional(),
  guide_id: z.string().uuid().optional(),
  max_pilgrims: z.number().int().positive().optional(),
  status: z.enum(['draft', 'active', 'completed', 'cancelled']).optional(),
});

/**
 * POST /api/v1/groups
 * Create a new group
 */
export async function createGroup(
  req: AuthRequest,
  res: Response
): Promise<void> {
  try {
    if (!req.user || !req.agency_id) {
      res.status(401).json({
        error: { code: 'UNAUTHORIZED', message: 'Authentication required' },
      });
      return;
    }

    const validationResult = groupCreateSchema.safeParse(req.body);

    if (!validationResult.success) {
      logger.warn({ errors: validationResult.error.errors }, 'Invalid group creation request');
      res.status(400).json({
        error: {
          code: 'VALIDATION_ERROR',
          message: 'Invalid input',
          details: { field_errors: validationResult.error.errors },
        },
      });
      return;
    }

    const input: GroupCreateInput = validationResult.data;

    // Verify guide exists and belongs to agency (if provided)
    if (input.guide_id) {
      const {  guide } = await supabase
        .from('users')
        .select('id, role')
        .eq('id', input.guide_id)
        .eq('agency_id', req.agency_id)
        .single();

      if (!guide) {
        res.status(400).json({
          error: { code: 'INVALID_GUIDE', message: 'Guide not found in your agency' },
        });
        return;
      }
    }

    const {  group, error } = await supabase
      .from('groups')
      .insert({
        agency_id: req.agency_id,
        ...input,
        status: 'draft',
      })
      .select()
      .single();

    if (error || !group) {
      logger.error({ error }, 'Failed to create group');
      res.status(500).json({
        error: {
          code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
          message: 'Failed to create group',
        },
      });
      return;
    }

    logger.info({
      groupId: group.id,
      agencyId: req.agency_id,
      userIdHash: hashEmail(req.user.email),
    }, 'Group created');

    res.status(201).json({ group });
  } catch (err) {
    logger.error({ error: err }, 'Create group error');
    res.status(500).json({
      error: {
        code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
        message: 'Failed to create group',
      },
    });
  }
}

/**
 * GET /api/v1/groups
 * List all groups for agency
 */
export async function listGroups(
  req: AuthRequest,
  res: Response
): Promise<void> {
  try {
    if (!req.user || !req.agency_id) {
      res.status(401).json({
        error: { code: 'UNAUTHORIZED', message: 'Authentication required' },
      });
      return;
    }

    const page = parseInt(req.query.page as string) || 1;
    const perPage = parseInt(req.query.per_page as string) || 20;
    const status = req.query.status as string;
    const search = req.query.search as string;

    let query = supabase
      .from('groups')
      .select('*', { count: 'exact' })
      .eq('agency_id', req.agency_id)
      .is('deleted_at', null)
      .order('created_at', { ascending: false });

    // Apply filters
    if (status) {
      query = query.eq('status', status);
    }

    if (search) {
      query = query.ilike('name', `%${search}%`);
    }

    // Pagination
    const from = (page - 1) * perPage;
    const to = from + perPage - 1;
    query = query.range(from, to);

    const {  groups, count, error } = await query;

    if (error) {
      logger.error({ error }, 'Failed to list groups');
      res.status(500).json({
        error: {
          code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
          message: 'Failed to list groups',
        },
      });
      return;
    }

    res.status(200).json({
      data: groups || [],
      pagination: {
        page,
        per_page: perPage,
        total: count || 0,
        total_pages: Math.ceil((count || 0) / perPage),
      },
    });
  } catch (err) {
    logger.error({ error: err }, 'List groups error');
    res.status(500).json({
      error: {
        code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
        message: 'Failed to list groups',
      },
    });
  }
}

/**
 * GET /api/v1/groups/:id
 * Get single group details
 */
export async function getGroup(
  req: AuthRequest,
  res: Response
): Promise<void> {
  try {
    if (!req.user || !req.agency_id) {
      res.status(401).json({
        error: { code: 'UNAUTHORIZED', message: 'Authentication required' },
      });
      return;
    }

    const groupId = req.params.id;

    const {  group } = await supabase
      .from('groups')
      .select(`
        *,
        guide:users!guide_id(id, first_name, last_name, email, phone),
        pilgrims_count:pilgrims(count),
        flights:flights(*),
        hotels:hotels(*)
      `)
      .eq('id', groupId)
      .eq('agency_id', req.agency_id)
      .is('deleted_at', null)
      .single();

    if (!group) {
      res.status(404).json({
        error: { code: 'NOT_FOUND', message: 'Group not found' },
      });
      return;
    }

    res.status(200).json({ group });
  } catch (err) {
    logger.error({ error: err }, 'Get group error');
    res.status(500).json({
      error: {
        code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
        message: 'Failed to get group',
      },
    });
  }
}

/**
 * PUT /api/v1/groups/:id
 * Update group
 */
export async function updateGroup(
  req: AuthRequest,
  res: Response
): Promise<void> {
  try {
    if (!req.user || !req.agency_id) {
      res.status(401).json({
        error: { code: 'UNAUTHORIZED', message: 'Authentication required' },
      });
      return;
    }

    const groupId = req.params.id;

    // Verify group exists and belongs to agency
    const {  existingGroup } = await supabase
      .from('groups')
      .select('id, agency_id')
      .eq('id', groupId)
      .eq('agency_id', req.agency_id)
      .is('deleted_at', null)
      .single();

    if (!existingGroup) {
      res.status(404).json({
        error: { code: 'NOT_FOUND', message: 'Group not found' },
      });
      return;
    }

    const validationResult = groupUpdateSchema.safeParse(req.body);

    if (!validationResult.success) {
      res.status(400).json({
        error: {
          code: 'VALIDATION_ERROR',
          message: 'Invalid input',
          details: { field_errors: validationResult.error.errors },
        },
      });
      return;
    }

    const input: GroupUpdateInput = validationResult.data;

    const {  group, error } = await supabase
      .from('groups')
      .update({
        ...input,
        updated_at: new Date().toISOString(),
      })
      .eq('id', groupId)
      .select()
      .single();

    if (error || !group) {
      logger.error({ error }, 'Failed to update group');
      res.status(500).json({
        error: {
          code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
          message: 'Failed to update group',
        },
      });
      return;
    }

    logger.info({
      groupId,
      agencyId: req.agency_id,
      userIdHash: hashEmail(req.user.email),
    }, 'Group updated');

    res.status(200).json({ group });
  } catch (err) {
    logger.error({ error: err }, 'Update group error');
    res.status(500).json({
      error: {
        code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
        message: 'Failed to update group',
      },
    });
  }
}

/**
 * DELETE /api/v1/groups/:id
 * Soft delete group
 */
export async function deleteGroup(
  req: AuthRequest,
  res: Response
): Promise<void> {
  try {
    if (!req.user || !req.agency_id) {
      res.status(401).json({
        error: { code: 'UNAUTHORIZED', message: 'Authentication required' },
      });
      return;
    }

    const groupId = req.params.id;

    // Soft delete
    const { error } = await supabase
      .from('groups')
      .update({
        deleted_at: new Date().toISOString(),
        updated_at: new Date().toISOString(),
      })
      .eq('id', groupId)
      .eq('agency_id', req.agency_id);

    if (error) {
      logger.error({ error }, 'Failed to delete group');
      res.status(500).json({
        error: {
          code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
          message: 'Failed to delete group',
        },
      });
      return;
    }

    logger.info({
      groupId,
      agencyId: req.agency_id,
      userIdHash: hashEmail(req.user.email),
    }, 'Group soft deleted');

    res.status(200).json({
      message: 'Group deleted successfully',
    });
  } catch (err) {
    logger.error({ error: err }, 'Delete group error');
    res.status(500).json({
      error: {
        code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
        message: 'Failed to delete group',
      },
    });
  }
}
```

### 📁 `packages/api/src/controllers/pilgrims.controller.ts`

```typescript
import { Response } from 'express';
import { z } from 'zod';
import pino from 'pino';
import { createClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js';
import { AuthRequest } from '../middleware/auth.js';
import { hashEmail } from '../utils/logger.js';
import { Pilgrim, PilgrimCreateInput, CsvImportResult } from '@mon-omra/shared';
import { parse } from 'csv-parse/sync';

const logger = pino({ level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info' });

const supabase = createClient(
  process.env.SUPABASE_URL!,
  process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!
);

// Validation schemas
const pilgrimCreateSchema = z.object({
  group_id: z.string().uuid().optional(),
  first_name: z.string().min(1).max(50),
  last_name: z.string().min(1).max(50),
  email: z.string().email().optional().or(z.literal('')),
  phone: z.string().optional(),
  birth_date: z.string().regex(/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/).optional(),
  gender: z.enum(['M', 'F']).optional(),
  passport_number: z.string().optional(),
  passport_expiry: z.string().regex(/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/).optional(),
});

const pilgrimUpdateSchema = pilgrimCreateSchema.partial();

const csvImportSchema = z.object({
  group_id: z.string().uuid(),
  csv_data: z.string(),
});

/**
 * POST /api/v1/pilgrims
 * Create a new pilgrim
 */
export async function createPilgrim(
  req: AuthRequest,
  res: Response
): Promise<void> {
  try {
    if (!req.user || !req.agency_id) {
      res.status(401).json({
        error: { code: 'UNAUTHORIZED', message: 'Authentication required' },
      });
      return;
    }

    const validationResult = pilgrimCreateSchema.safeParse(req.body);

    if (!validationResult.success) {
      res.status(400).json({
        error: {
          code: 'VALIDATION_ERROR',
          message: 'Invalid input',
          details: { field_errors: validationResult.error.errors },
        },
      });
      return;
    }

    const input: PilgrimCreateInput = validationResult.data;

    // Verify group exists and belongs to agency (if provided)
    if (input.group_id) {
      const {  group } = await supabase
        .from('groups')
        .select('id')
        .eq('id', input.group_id)
        .eq('agency_id', req.agency_id)
        .is('deleted_at', null)
        .single();

      if (!group) {
        res.status(400).json({
          error: { code: 'INVALID_GROUP', message: 'Group not found in your agency' },
        });
        return;
      }
    }

    const {  pilgrim, error } = await supabase
      .from('pilgrims')
      .insert({
        agency_id: req.agency_id,
        ...input,
      })
      .select()
      .single();

    if (error || !pilgrim) {
      logger.error({ error }, 'Failed to create pilgrim');
      res.status(500).json({
        error: {
          code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
          message: 'Failed to create pilgrim',
        },
      });
      return;
    }

    logger.info({
      pilgrimId: pilgrim.id,
      agencyId: req.agency_id,
      userIdHash: hashEmail(req.user.email),
    }, 'Pilgrim created');

    res.status(201).json({ pilgrim });
  } catch (err) {
    logger.error({ error: err }, 'Create pilgrim error');
    res.status(500).json({
      error: {
        code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
        message: 'Failed to create pilgrim',
      },
    });
  }
}

/**
 * POST /api/v1/pilgrims/import
 * Import pilgrims from CSV
 */
export async function importPilgrims(
  req: AuthRequest,
  res: Response
): Promise<void> {
  try {
    if (!req.user || !req.agency_id) {
      res.status(401).json({
        error: { code: 'UNAUTHORIZED', message: 'Authentication required' },
      });
      return;
    }

    const validationResult = csvImportSchema.safeParse(req.body);

    if (!validationResult.success) {
      res.status(400).json({
        error: {
          code: 'VALIDATION_ERROR',
          message: 'Invalid input',
          details: { field_errors: validationResult.error.errors },
        },
      });
      return;
    }

    const { group_id, csv_data } = validationResult.data;

    // Verify group exists
    const {  group } = await supabase
      .from('groups')
      .select('id')
      .eq('id', group_id)
      .eq('agency_id', req.agency_id)
      .single();

    if (!group) {
      res.status(400).json({
        error: { code: 'INVALID_GROUP', message: 'Group not found' },
      });
      return;
    }

    // Parse CSV
    const records = parse(csv_data, {
      columns: true,
      skip_empty_lines: true,
      trim: true,
    });

    const result: CsvImportResult = {
      total: records.length,
      success: 0,
      failed: 0,
      errors: [],
      imported_pilgrims: [],
    };

    // Process each row
    for (let i = 0; i < records.length; i++) {
      const row = records[i];
      const rowNum = i + 2; // 1-indexed + header

      try {
        // Validate row
        const validated = pilgrimCreateSchema.parse({
          group_id,
          first_name: row.first_name || row.firstName || row['Prénom'],
          last_name: row.last_name || row.lastName || row['Nom'],
          email: row.email || row.Email,
          phone: row.phone || row.Phone || row['Téléphone'],
          birth_date: row.birth_date || row.birthDate || row['Date naissance'],
          gender: row.gender || row.Gender || row['Sexe'],
          passport_number: row.passport_number || row.passportNumber || row['Passeport'],
          passport_expiry: row.passport_expiry || row.passportExpiry || row['Expiration passeport'],
        });

        // Insert pilgrim
        const {  pilgrim, error } = await supabase
          .from('pilgrims')
          .insert({
            agency_id: req.agency_id,
            ...validated,
          })
          .select('id, email')
          .single();

        if (error || !pilgrim) {
          throw new Error(error?.message || 'Insert failed');
        }

        result.success++;
        result.imported_pilgrims.push({ id: pilgrim.id, email: pilgrim.email });
      } catch (err) {
        result.failed++;
        result.errors.push({
          row: rowNum,
          message: err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Unknown error',
           row,
        });
      }
    }

    logger.info({
      groupId: group_id,
      total: result.total,
      success: result.success,
      failed: result.failed,
      userIdHash: hashEmail(req.user.email),
    }, 'Pilgrims CSV import completed');

    res.status(200).json({
      message: 'Import completed',
      ...result,
    });
  } catch (err) {
    logger.error({ error: err }, 'Import pilgrims error');
    res.status(500).json({
      error: {
        code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
        message: 'Failed to import pilgrims',
      },
    });
  }
}

/**
 * GET /api/v1/pilgrims
 * List pilgrims for agency
 */
export async function listPilgrims(
  req: AuthRequest,
  res: Response
): Promise<void> {
  try {
    if (!req.user || !req.agency_id) {
      res.status(401).json({
        error: { code: 'UNAUTHORIZED', message: 'Authentication required' },
      });
      return;
    }

    const page = parseInt(req.query.page as string) || 1;
    const perPage = parseInt(req.query.per_page as string) || 50;
    const group_id = req.query.group_id as string;
    const search = req.query.search as string;

    let query = supabase
      .from('pilgrims')
      .select('*', { count: 'exact' })
      .eq('agency_id', req.agency_id)
      .is('deleted_at', null)
      .order('created_at', { ascending: false });

    if (group_id) {
      query = query.eq('group_id', group_id);
    }

    if (search) {
      query = query.or(`first_name.ilike.%${search}%,last_name.ilike.%${search}%,email.ilike.%${search}%`);
    }

    const from = (page - 1) * perPage;
    const to = from + perPage - 1;
    query = query.range(from, to);

    const {  pilgrims, count, error } = await query;

    if (error) {
      logger.error({ error }, 'Failed to list pilgrims');
      res.status(500).json({
        error: {
          code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
          message: 'Failed to list pilgrims',
        },
      });
      return;
    }

    res.status(200).json({
       pilgrims || [],
      pagination: {
        page,
        per_page: perPage,
        total: count || 0,
        total_pages: Math.ceil((count || 0) / perPage),
      },
    });
  } catch (err) {
    logger.error({ error: err }, 'List pilgrims error');
    res.status(500).json({
      error: {
        code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
        message: 'Failed to list pilgrims',
      },
    });
  }
}

/**
 * PUT /api/v1/pilgrims/:id
 * Update pilgrim
 */
export async function updatePilgrim(
  req: AuthRequest,
  res: Response
): Promise<void> {
  try {
    if (!req.user || !req.agency_id) {
      res.status(401).json({
        error: { code: 'UNAUTHORIZED', message: 'Authentication required' },
      });
      return;
    }

    const pilgrimId = req.params.id;

    const validationResult = pilgrimUpdateSchema.safeParse(req.body);

    if (!validationResult.success) {
      res.status(400).json({
        error: {
          code: 'VALIDATION_ERROR',
          message: 'Invalid input',
          details: { field_errors: validationResult.error.errors },
        },
      });
      return;
    }

    const input = validationResult.data;

    const {  pilgrim, error } = await supabase
      .from('pilgrims')
      .update({
        ...input,
        updated_at: new Date().toISOString(),
      })
      .eq('id', pilgrimId)
      .eq('agency_id', req.agency_id)
      .select()
      .single();

    if (error || !pilgrim) {
      res.status(404).json({
        error: { code: 'NOT_FOUND', message: 'Pilgrim not found' },
      });
      return;
    }

    logger.info({
      pilgrimId,
      agencyId: req.agency_id,
      userIdHash: hashEmail(req.user.email),
    }, 'Pilgrim updated');

    res.status(200).json({ pilgrim });
  } catch (err) {
    logger.error({ error: err }, 'Update pilgrim error');
    res.status(500).json({
      error: {
        code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
        message: 'Failed to update pilgrim',
      },
    });
  }
}

/**
 * DELETE /api/v1/pilgrims/:id
 * Soft delete pilgrim
 */
export async function deletePilgrim(
  req: AuthRequest,
  res: Response
): Promise<void> {
  try {
    if (!req.user || !req.agency_id) {
      res.status(401).json({
        error: { code: 'UNAUTHORIZED', message: 'Authentication required' },
      });
      return;
    }

    const pilgrimId = req.params.id;

    const { error } = await supabase
      .from('pilgrims')
      .update({
        deleted_at: new Date().toISOString(),
        updated_at: new Date().toISOString(),
      })
      .eq('id', pilgrimId)
      .eq('agency_id', req.agency_id);

    if (error) {
      res.status(500).json({
        error: {
          code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
          message: 'Failed to delete pilgrim',
        },
      });
      return;
    }

    logger.info({
      pilgrimId,
      agencyId: req.agency_id,
      userIdHash: hashEmail(req.user.email),
    }, 'Pilgrim soft deleted');

    res.status(200).json({
      message: 'Pilgrim deleted successfully',
    });
  } catch (err) {
    logger.error({ error: err }, 'Delete pilgrim error');
    res.status(500).json({
      error: {
        code: 'INTERNAL_ERROR',
        message: 'Failed to delete pilgrim',
      },
    });
  }
}
```

### 📁 `packages/web/app/backoffice/groups/page.tsx`

```typescript
'use client';

import { useState } from 'react';
import { useQuery, useMutation, useQueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { apiClient } from '@/lib/api';
import { Group } from '@mon-omra/shared';
import { CreateGroupModal } from './components/CreateGroupModal';
import { GroupTable } from './components/GroupTable';
import { Pagination } from '@/components/Pagination';
import { PlusIcon, SearchIcon } from '@/components/icons';

interface GroupsResponse {
   Group[];
  pagination: {
    page: number;
    per_page: number;
    total: number;
    total_pages: number;
  };
}

export default function GroupsPage() {
  const [page, setPage] = useState(1);
  const [search, setSearch] = useState('');
  const [status, setStatus] = useState<string>('');
  const [isCreateModalOpen, setIsCreateModalOpen] = useState(false);
  const queryClient = useQueryClient();

  const { data, isLoading, error } = useQuery<GroupsResponse>({
    queryKey: ['groups', page, search, status],
    queryFn: async () => {
      const params = new URLSearchParams({
        page: page.toString(),
        per_page: '20',
        ...(search && { search }),
        ...(status && { status }),
      });
      const response = await apiClient.get(`/api/v1/groups?${params}`);
      return response;
    },
  });

  const createGroupMutation = useMutation({
    mutationFn: async (groupData: Partial<Group>) => {
      const response = await apiClient.post('/api/v1/groups', groupData);
      return response;
    },
    onSuccess: () => {
      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['groups'] });
      setIsCreateModalOpen(false);
    },
  });

  const handleCreateGroup = (groupData: Partial<Group>) => {
    createGroupMutation.mutate(groupData);
  };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-50">
      {/* Header */}
      <header className="bg-white border-b border-gray-200">
        <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto px-4 py-6">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
            <div>
              <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900">
                Gestion des groupes
              </h1>
              <p className="text-sm text-gray-600 mt-1">
                Créez et gérez vos groupes de pèlerins
              </p>
            </div>
            <button
              onClick={() => setIsCreateModalOpen(true)}
              className="inline-flex items-center px-4 py-2 bg-emerald-600 text-white font-medium rounded-lg hover:bg-emerald-700 transition-colors focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-500 focus:ring-offset-2"
            >
              <PlusIcon className="w-5 h-5 mr-2" />
              Nouveau groupe
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </header>

      {/* Filters */}
      <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto px-4 py-4">
        <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row gap-4">
          <div className="flex-1 relative">
            <SearchIcon className="w-5 h-5 absolute left-3 top-1/2 transform -translate-y-1/2 text-gray-400" />
            <input
              type="text"
              placeholder="Rechercher un groupe..."
              value={search}
              onChange={(e) => setSearch(e.target.value)}
              className="w-full pl-10 pr-4 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-500 focus:border-emerald-500"
            />
          </div>
          <select
            value={status}
            onChange={(e) => setStatus(e.target.value)}
            className="px-4 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-500 focus:border-emerald-500"
          >
            <option value="">Tous les statuts</option>
            <option value="draft">Brouillon</option>
            <option value="active">Actif</option>
            <option value="completed">Terminé</option>
            <option value="cancelled">Annulé</option>
          </select>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Content */}
      <main className="max-w-7xl mx-auto px-4 py-6">
        {isLoading ? (
          <div className="bg-white rounded-xl border border-gray-200 p-8 text-center">
            <div className="animate-pulse space-y-4">
              <div className="h-4 bg-gray-200 rounded w-3/4 mx-auto" />
              <div className="h-4 bg-gray-200 rounded w-1/2 mx-auto" />
            </div>
          </div>
        ) : error ? (
          <div className="bg-red-50 border border-red-200 rounded-xl p-6 text-red-900">
            Erreur lors du chargement des groupes. Veuillez réessayer.
          </div>
        ) : (
          <>
            <GroupTable groups={data?.data || []} />
            
            {data && data.pagination.total_pages > 1 && (
              <Pagination
                currentPage={page}
                totalPages={data.pagination.total_pages}
                onPageChange={setPage}
              />
            )}
          </>
        )}
      </main>

      {/* Create Modal */}
      {isCreateModalOpen && (
        <CreateGroupModal
          onClose={() => setIsCreateModalOpen(false)}
          onSubmit={handleCreateGroup}
          isLoading={createGroupMutation.isPending}
        />
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
```

### 📁 `packages/web/app/backoffice/groups/components/CreateGroupModal.tsx`

```typescript
'use client';

import { useState } from 'react';
import { useForm } from 'react-hook-form';
import { zodResolver } from '@hookform/resolvers/zod';
import { z } from 'zod';
import { XIcon } from '@/components/icons';

const groupSchema = z.object({
  name: z.string().min(2, 'Le nom doit contenir au moins 2 caractères'),
  departure_date: z.string().regex(/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/, 'Date invalide'),
  return_date: z.string().regex(/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/, 'Date invalide').optional(),
  max_pilgrims: z.number().int().positive().optional(),
});

type GroupFormData = z.infer<typeof groupSchema>;

interface CreateGroupModalProps {
  onClose: () => void;
  onSubmit: (data: Partial<GroupFormData>) => void;
  isLoading: boolean;
}

export function CreateGroupModal({ onClose, onSubmit, isLoading }: CreateGroupModalProps) {
  const {
    register,
    handleSubmit,
    formState: { errors },
  } = useForm<GroupFormData>({
    resolver: zodResolver(groupSchema),
  });

  const handleSubmitForm = ( GroupFormData) => {
    onSubmit(data);
  };

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 overflow-y-auto">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-center min-h-screen px-4 pt-4 pb-20 text-center sm:p-0">
        {/* Backdrop */}
        <div
          className="fixed inset-0 transition-opacity bg-gray-500 bg-opacity-75"
          onClick={onClose}
        />

        {/* Modal */}
        <div className="inline-block w-full max-w-md p-6 my-8 overflow-hidden text-left align-middle transition-all transform bg-white shadow-xl rounded-2xl">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-6">
            <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900">
              Créer un nouveau groupe
            </h3>
            <button
              onClick={onClose}
              className="text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-600"
            >
              <XIcon className="w-6 h-6" />
            </button>
          </div>

          <form onSubmit={handleSubmit(handleSubmitForm)} className="space-y-4">
            <div>
              <label htmlFor="name" className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">
                Nom du groupe *
              </label>
              <input
                id="name"
                type="text"
                {...register('name')}
                className="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-500 focus:border-emerald-500"
                placeholder="Ex: Omra Avril 2025"
              />
              {errors.name && (
                <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-red-600">{errors.name.message}</p>
              )}
            </div>

            <div>
              <label htmlFor="departure_date" className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">
                Date de départ *
              </label>
              <input
                id="departure_date"
                type="date"
                {...register('departure_date')}
                className="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-500 focus:border-emerald-500"
              />
              {errors.departure_date && (
                <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-red-600">{errors.departure_date.message}</p>
              )}
            </div>

            <div>
              <label htmlFor="return_date" className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">
                Date de retour
              </label>
              <input
                id="return_date"
                type="date"
                {...register('return_date')}
                className="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-500 focus:border-emerald-500"
              />
              {errors.return_date && (
                <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-red-600">{errors.return_date.message}</p>
              )}
            </div>

            <div>
              <label htmlFor="max_pilgrims" className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">
                Nombre maximum de pèlerins
              </label>
              <input
                id="max_pilgrims"
                type="number"
                {...register('max_pilgrims', { valueAsNumber: true })}
                className="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-500 focus:border-emerald-500"
                placeholder="Ex: 50"
              />
              {errors.max_pilgrims && (
                <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-red-600">{errors.max_pilgrims.message}</p>
              )}
            </div>

            <div className="flex gap-3 pt-4">
              <button
                type="button"
                onClick={onClose}
                className="flex-1 px-4 py-2 border border-gray-300 text-gray-700 font-medium rounded-lg hover:bg-gray-50 transition-colors"
              >
                Annuler
              </button>
              <button
                type="submit"
                disabled={isLoading}
                className="flex-1 px-4 py-2 bg-emerald-600 text-white font-medium rounded-lg hover:bg-emerald-700 transition-colors disabled:opacity-50"
              >
                {isLoading ? 'Création...' : 'Créer le groupe'}
              </button>
            </div>
          </form>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

### 📁 `packages/api/src/routes/backoffice.routes.ts`

```typescript
import { Router } from 'express';
import {
  createGroup,
  listGroups,
  getGroup,
  updateGroup,
  deleteGroup,
} from '../controllers/groups.controller.js';
import {
  createPilgrim,
  importPilgrims,
  listPilgrims,
  updatePilgrim,
  deletePilgrim,
} from '../controllers/pilgrims.controller.js';
import { authMiddleware, requireRoles } from '../middleware/auth.js';
import { apiRateLimit } from '../middleware/rate-limit.js';

const router = Router();

// All backoffice routes require authentication
router.use(authMiddleware);
router.use(apiRateLimit());

// Groups routes
router.post('/groups', requireRoles('super_admin', 'ops'), createGroup);
router.get('/groups', listGroups);
router.get('/groups/:id', getGroup);
router.put('/groups/:id', requireRoles('super_admin', 'ops'), updateGroup);
router.delete('/groups/:id', requireRoles('super_admin', 'ops'), deleteGroup);

// Pilgrims routes
router.post('/pilgrims', requireRoles('super_admin', 'ops'), createPilgrim);
router.post('/pilgrims/import', requireRoles('super_admin', 'ops'), importPilgrims);
router.get('/pilgrims', listPilgrims);
router.put('/pilgrims/:id', requireRoles('super_admin', 'ops'), updatePilgrim);
router.delete('/pilgrims/:id', requireRoles('super_admin', 'ops'), deletePilgrim);

// Flights routes (similar structure)
// router.post('/flights', requireRoles('super_admin', 'ops'), createFlight);
// router.get('/flights', listFlights);
// ...

// Hotels routes (similar structure)
// router.post('/hotels', requireRoles('super_admin', 'ops'), createHotel);
// router.get('/hotels', listHotels);
// ...

export default router;
```

### 📁 `packages/api/tests/backoffice.test.ts`

```typescript
import { describe, it, expect, beforeAll } from 'vitest';
import request from 'supertest';
import { app } from '../src/app.js';
import { supabase } from './utils/supabase-test.js';

describe('Back-Office Module', () => {
  let agencyToken: string;
  let groupId: string;
  let pilgrimId: string;

  beforeAll(async () => {
    agencyToken = await getTestUserToken('ops@agency-a.local');
  });

  describe('Groups CRUD', () => {
    it('should create a new group', async () => {
      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/v1/groups')
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${agencyToken}`)
        .send({
          name: 'Test Group 2025',
          departure_date: '2025-04-15',
          return_date: '2025-04-25',
          max_pilgrims: 50,
        });

      expect(response.status).toBe(201);
      expect(response.body.group.name).toBe('Test Group 2025');
      groupId = response.body.group.id;
    });

    it('should list groups for agency', async () => {
      const response = await request(app)
        .get('/api/v1/groups')
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${agencyToken}`);

      expect(response.status).toBe(200);
      expect(Array.isArray(response.body.data)).toBe(true);
    });

    it('should get single group', async () => {
      const response = await request(app)
        .get(`/api/v1/groups/${groupId}`)
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${agencyToken}`);

      expect(response.status).toBe(200);
      expect(response.body.group.id).toBe(groupId);
    });

    it('should update group', async () => {
      const response = await request(app)
        .put(`/api/v1/groups/${groupId}`)
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${agencyToken}`)
        .send({
          name: 'Updated Group Name',
        });

      expect(response.status).toBe(200);
      expect(response.body.group.name).toBe('Updated Group Name');
    });

    it('should soft delete group', async () => {
      const response = await request(app)
        .delete(`/api/v1/groups/${groupId}`)
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${agencyToken}`);

      expect(response.status).toBe(200);
      expect(response.body.message).toContain('deleted');
    });

    it('should reject pilgrim role from creating group', async () => {
      const pilgrimToken = await getTestUserToken('pilgrim@agency-a.local');
      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/v1/groups')
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${pilgrimToken}`)
        .send({
          name: 'Invalid Group',
          departure_date: '2025-04-15',
        });

      expect(response.status).toBe(403);
      expect(response.body.error.code).toBe('FORBIDDEN');
    });
  });

  describe('Pilgrims CRUD', () => {
    it('should create a new pilgrim', async () => {
      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/v1/pilgrims')
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${agencyToken}`)
        .send({
          first_name: 'Ahmed',
          last_name: 'Benali',
          email: 'ahmed.test@monomra-test.local',
        });

      expect(response.status).toBe(201);
      expect(response.body.pilgrim.first_name).toBe('Ahmed');
      pilgrimId = response.body.pilgrim.id;
    });

    it('should list pilgrims for agency', async () => {
      const response = await request(app)
        .get('/api/v1/pilgrims')
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${agencyToken}`);

      expect(response.status).toBe(200);
      expect(Array.isArray(response.body.data)).toBe(true);
    });

    it('should import pilgrims from CSV', async () => {
      const csvData = `first_name,last_name,email,birth_date
John,Doe,john@test.local,1990-01-15
Jane,Smith,jane@test.local,1985-03-20`;

      // First create a group for import
      const groupResponse = await request(app)
        .post('/api/v1/groups')
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${agencyToken}`)
        .send({
          name: 'Import Test Group',
          departure_date: '2025-05-01',
        });

      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/v1/pilgrims/import')
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${agencyToken}`)
        .send({
          group_id: groupResponse.body.group.id,
          csv_ csvData,
        });

      expect(response.status).toBe(200);
      expect(response.body.total).toBe(2);
      expect(response.body.success).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(0);
    });
  });
});

async function getTestUserToken(email: string): Promise<string> {
  const { data } = await supabase.auth.signInWithOtp({ email });
  return data?.session?.access_token || '';
}
```

## 4) Top 5 Risques Résiduels + Mitigations

| Risque | Impact | Mitigation | Statut |
|--------|--------|------------|--------|
| **Bug critique non détecté en prod** | Élevé | Feature flags + rollback automatique + monitoring | ✅ Mitigé |
| **Charge utilisateur > prévisions** | Moyen | Auto-scaling Supabase + cache Redis P1 | ⚠️ À monitorer |
| **Emails en spam** | Moyen | Domain authentication (DKIM/SPF) + warm-up | ✅ Configuré |
| **Erreur humaine suppression données** | Élevé | Soft delete + backups quotidiens + confirmation modale | ✅ Mitigé |
| **Non-conformité RGPD découverte post-launch** | Critique | Audit trimestriel + DPO accessible + DSAR testé | ✅ Documenté |
